"angular","TITLE: Serve Angular Examples with Bazel
DESCRIPTION: Commands to serve individual Angular example applications using Bazel. This allows developers to run specific examples locally for testing application behavior.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/packages/examples/README.md#_snippet_0

LANGUAGE: shell
CODE:
```
# Serving individual examples (e.g. common)
yarn bazel run //packages/examples/common:devserver

# ""core"" examples
yarn bazel run //packages/examples/core:devserver
```

TITLE: TestabilityRegistry API
DESCRIPTION: Manages the registration and retrieval of testability instances for Angular applications. Provides methods to find testability in the DOM tree, get all root elements, and manage application registrations.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/core/index.api.md#_snippet_93

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
TestabilityRegistry:
  findTestabilityInTree(elem: Node, findInAncestors?: boolean): Testability | null;
    - Finds the Testability instance associated with a DOM element or its ancestors.
    - Parameters:
      - elem: The DOM Node to start searching from.
      - findInAncestors: If true, searches up the DOM tree for a testability instance.
    - Returns: The Testability instance or null if not found.

  getAllRootElements(): any[];
    - Retrieves all root DOM elements associated with registered Angular applications.
    - Returns: An array of root elements.

  getAllTestabilities(): Testability[];
    - Retrieves all registered Testability instances.
    - Returns: An array of Testability instances.

  getTestability(elem: any): Testability | null;
    - Retrieves the Testability instance for a specific DOM element.
    - Parameters:
      - elem: The DOM element.
    - Returns: The Testability instance or null.

  registerApplication(token: any, testability: Testability): void;
    - Registers a new testability instance with a unique token.
    - Parameters:
      - token: A unique identifier for the application.
      - testability: The Testability instance to register.

  unregisterAllApplications(): void;
    - Unregisters all previously registered applications.

  unregisterApplication(token: any): void;
    - Unregisters a specific application using its token.
    - Parameters:
      - token: The token of the application to unregister.
```

TITLE: Server-Side AI Response Streaming with Gemini API
DESCRIPTION: Provides a server-side example using Node.js and Express to stream AI responses. It connects to the Gemini API, retrieves content stream, and writes each text chunk to the response object. This pattern is applicable to other LLM streaming APIs.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/ai/overview.md#_snippet_12

LANGUAGE: ts
CODE:
```
app.get(""/api/stream-response"", async (req, res) => {
   ai.models.generateContentStream({
     model: ""gemini-2.0-flash"",
     contents: ""Explain how AI works"",
   }).then(async (response) => {
     for await (const chunk of response) {
       res.write(chunk.text);
     }
   });
 });
```

----------------------------------------

TITLE: Browser View Transitions API Example
DESCRIPTION: Demonstrates the basic usage of the browser's native `document.startViewTransition` API. This method captures the current DOM state, allows for DOM updates within a callback, and then captures the new state to create a visual transition.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/guide/animations/route-animations.md#_snippet_0

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
document.startViewTransition(callback: () => Promise<void> | void)
  - Captures the current DOM state before executing the callback.
  - The callback function updates the DOM and can be asynchronous.
  - The browser captures the new DOM state after the callback promise resolves.
  - Initiates the visual transition between the old and new DOM states.
  - Example:
    document.startViewTransition(async () => {
      await updateTheDOMSomehow();
    });
```

----------------------------------------

TITLE: Web Animations API Events
DESCRIPTION: Lists common events available in the Web Animations API for tracking animation and transition lifecycles. These include start, end, iteration, and cancel events for both animations and transitions.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/guide/animations/css.md#_snippet_14

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Animation Events:
  - animationstart: Fired when an animation starts.
  - animationend: Fired when an animation completes.
  - animationiteration: Fired when an animation repeats.
  - animationcancel: Fired when an animation is cancelled.

Transition Events:
  - transitionstart: Fired when a CSS transition starts.
  - transitionrun: Fired when a CSS transition begins its execution.
  - transitionend: Fired when a CSS transition completes.
  - transitioncancel: Fired when a CSS transition is cancelled.

Note: Be mindful of event bubbling. Examine `animationname` or transitioned properties to identify the correct event target.
```

TITLE: TransferState API
DESCRIPTION: Provides a mechanism for transferring application state between server and client during Angular Universal rendering. Allows setting, getting, and checking for keys in the state.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/core/index.api.md#_snippet_94

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
TransferState:
  get<T>(key: StateKey<T>, defaultValue: T): T;
    - Retrieves the value associated with a StateKey, returning a default value if not found.
    - Parameters:
      - key: The StateKey to look up.
      - defaultValue: The value to return if the key is not present.
    - Returns: The value for the key or the defaultValue.

  hasKey<T>(key: StateKey<T>): boolean;
    - Checks if a StateKey exists in the transfer state.
    - Parameters:
      - key: The StateKey to check.
    - Returns: True if the key exists, false otherwise.

  isEmpty(): boolean;
    - Checks if the transfer state is empty.
    - Returns: True if no state has been set, false otherwise.

  onSerialize<T>(key: StateKey<T>, callback: () => T): void;
    - Registers a callback to serialize a value for a given StateKey when the state is serialized to JSON.
    - Parameters:
      - key: The StateKey for which to register the callback.
      - callback: A function that returns the value to be serialized.

  remove<T>(key: StateKey<T>): void;
    - Removes a StateKey and its associated value from the transfer state.
    - Parameters:
      - key: The StateKey to remove.

  set<T>(key: StateKey<T>, value: T): void;
    - Sets a value for a given StateKey in the transfer state.
    - Parameters:
      - key: The StateKey to set.
      - value: The value to associate with the key.

  toJson(): string;
    - Serializes the current transfer state into a JSON string.
```

LANGUAGE: ts
CODE:
```
import { HttpClient } from '@angular/common/http';

// Assume 'http' is an instance of HttpClient injected into your component/service
// Assume 'Config' is a defined interface for the expected JSON structure

http.get<Config>('/api/config').subscribe(config => {
  // Process the configuration data received from the server.
  console.log('Configuration loaded:', config);
});

TITLE: Angular Core Component API Reference
DESCRIPTION: API documentation for the core Angular `Component` decorator and its associated metadata. This reference details how to define and configure components in Angular applications.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/tutorials/first-app/steps/02-Home/README.md#_snippet_8

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Component decorator

Description:
  Decorator that marks a class as an Angular component and provides configuration metadata that determines its view, data binding, and other features.

Usage:
  @Component({...})
  class MyComponent {...}

Metadata Properties:
  selector: string | string[]
    A CSS selector that identifies this component in a template.
    Example: 'app-my-component'

  template: string
    An inline template for the component.
    Example: '<h1>Hello</h1>'

  templateUrl: string
    The URL to a template file for the component.
    Example: './my-component.component.html'

  styles: string[]
    An array of inline styles for the component.
    Example: ['.host { color: red; }']

  styleUrls: string[]
    An array of URLs to stylesheet files for the component.
    Example: ['./my-component.component.css']

  providers: any[]
    An array of dependency injection providers for this component.

  changeDetection: ChangeDetectionStrategy
    Specifies the change detection strategy (OnPush or Default).

  viewEncapsulation: ViewEncapsulation
    Specifies the view encapsulation strategy (Emulated, None, or ShadowDom).

Example:
  @Component({
    selector: 'app-user-profile',
    templateUrl: './user-profile.component.html',
    styleUrls: ['./user-profile.component.css'],
    providers: [UserService]
  })
  export class UserProfileComponent {
    // Component logic
  }

Related Concepts:
  Angular Modules
  Directives
  Services
```

TITLE: Angular Server Rendering API
DESCRIPTION: Provides core functions for server-side rendering of Angular applications and modules. Includes methods to create platform references, render applications to strings, and configure server rendering.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/platform-server/index.api.md#_snippet_0

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Angular Server Rendering Functions:

platformServer(extraProviders?: StaticProvider[] | undefined): PlatformRef
  - Creates a platform reference for server-side rendering.
  - Parameters:
    - extraProviders: Optional static providers to configure the platform.
  - Returns: A PlatformRef instance.

provideServerRendering(): EnvironmentProviders
  - Provides the necessary environment providers for server-side rendering.
  - Returns: An EnvironmentProviders object.

renderApplication<T>(bootstrap: () => Promise<ApplicationRef>, options: { document?: string | Document; url?: string; platformProviders?: Provider[]; }): Promise<string>
  - Renders an Angular application to a string.
  - Parameters:
    - bootstrap: A function that returns a Promise resolving to the ApplicationRef.
    - options: Configuration options including document, URL, and platform providers.
  - Returns: A Promise that resolves to the rendered HTML string.

renderModule<T>(moduleType: Type<T>, options: { document?: string | Document; url?: string; extraProviders?: StaticProvider[]; }): Promise<string>
  - Renders an Angular module to a string.
  - Parameters:
    - moduleType: The root Angular module type to render.
    - options: Configuration options including document, URL, and extra providers.
  - Returns: A Promise that resolves to the rendered HTML string.
```

TITLE: Angular HttpClient GET Method Overloads

    reportProgress?: boolean;
    responseType: 'arraybuffer';
    withCredentials?: boolean;
    credentials?: RequestCredentials;
    keepalive?: boolean;
    priority?: RequestPriority;
    cache?: RequestCache;
    mode?: RequestMode;
    redirect?: RequestRedirect;
    referrer?: string;
    integrity?: string;
    transferCache?: {
        includeHeaders?: string[];
    } | boolean;
    timeout?: number;
}): Observable<ArrayBuffer>;
```

TITLE: Angular HttpClient GET Method Overloads
DESCRIPTION: Documents the overloaded 'get' method of Angular's HttpClient service. It allows fetching resources from a URL with configurable options for headers, response types, progress events, and more. Each overload specifies the expected return type based on the 'responseType' and 'observe' options.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/common/http/index.api.md#_snippet_6

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
HttpClient.get

Fetches a resource from a given URL.

Overloads:

1.  get(url: string, options: {
        headers?: HttpHeaders | Record<string, string | string[]>;
        observe: 'events';
        context?: HttpContext;
        params?: HttpParams | Record<string, string | number | boolean | ReadonlyArray<string | number | boolean>>;
        reportProgress?: boolean;
        responseType: 'arraybuffer';
        withCredentials?: boolean;
        credentials?: RequestCredentials;
        keepalive?: boolean;
        priority?: RequestPriority;
        cache?: RequestCache;
        mode?: RequestMode;
        redirect?: RequestRedirect;
        referrer?: string;
        integrity?: string;
        transferCache?: {
            includeHeaders?: string[];
        } | boolean;
        timeout?: number;
    }): Observable<HttpEvent<ArrayBuffer>>;

2.  get(url: string, options: {
        headers?: HttpHeaders | Record<string, string | string[]>;
        observe: 'events';
        context?: HttpContext;
        params?: HttpParams | Record<string, string | number | boolean | ReadonlyArray<string | number | boolean>>;
        reportProgress?: boolean;
        responseType: 'blob';
        withCredentials?: boolean;
        credentials?: RequestCredentials;
        keepalive?: boolean;
        priority?: RequestPriority;
        cache?: RequestCache;
        mode?: RequestMode;
        redirect?: RequestRedirect;
        referrer?: string;
        integrity?: string;
        transferCache?: {
            includeHeaders?: string[];
        } | boolean;
        timeout?: number;
    }): Observable<HttpEvent<Blob>>;

3.  get(url: string, options: {
        headers?: HttpHeaders | Record<string, string | string[]>;
        observe: 'events';
        context?: HttpContext;
        params?: HttpParams | Record<string, string | number | boolean | ReadonlyArray<string | number | boolean>>;
        reportProgress?: boolean;
        responseType: 'text';
        withCredentials?: boolean;
        credentials?: RequestCredentials;
        keepalive?: boolean;
        priority?: RequestPriority;
        cache?: RequestCache;
        mode?: RequestMode;
        redirect?: RequestRedirect;
        referrer?: string;
        integrity?: string;
        transferCache?: {
            includeHeaders?: string[];
        } | boolean;
        timeout?: number;
    }): Observable<HttpEvent<string>>;

4.  get(url: string, options: {
        headers?: HttpHeaders | Record<string, string | string[]>;
        observe: 'events';
        context?: HttpContext;
        params?: HttpParams | Record<string, string | number | boolean | ReadonlyArray<string | number | boolean>>;
        reportProgress?: boolean;
        responseType?: 'json';
        withCredentials?: boolean;
        credentials?: RequestCredentials;
        keepalive?: boolean;
        priority?: RequestPriority;
        cache?: RequestCache;
        mode?: RequestMode;
        redirect?: RequestRedirect;
        referrer?: string;
        integrity?: string;
        transferCache?: {
            includeHeaders?: string[];
        } | boolean;
        timeout?: number;
    }): Observable<HttpEvent<Object>>;

5.  get<T>(url: string, options: {
        headers?: HttpHeaders | Record<string, string | string[]>;
        observe: 'events';
        context?: HttpContext;
        params?: HttpParams | Record<string, string | number | boolean | ReadonlyArray<string | number | boolean>>;
        reportProgress?: boolean;
        responseType?: 'json';
        withCredentials?: boolean;
        credentials?: RequestCredentials;
        keepalive?: boolean;
        priority?: RequestPriority;
        cache?: RequestCache;
        mode?: RequestMode;
        redirect?: RequestRedirect;
        referrer?: string;
        integrity?: string;
        transferCache?: {
            includeHeaders?: string[];
        } | boolean;
        timeout?: number;
    }): Observable<HttpEvent<T>>;

6.  get(url: string, options: {
        headers?: HttpHeaders | Record<string, string | string[]>;
        observe: 'response';
        context?: HttpContext;
        params?: HttpParams | Record<string, string | number | boolean | ReadonlyArray<string | number | boolean>>;
        reportProgress?: boolean;
        responseType: 'arraybuffer';
        withCredentials?: boolean;
        credentials?: RequestCredentials;
        keepalive?: boolean;
        priority?: RequestPriority;
        cache?: RequestCache;
        mode?: RequestMode;
        redirect?: RequestRedirect;
        referrer?: string;
        integrity?: string;
        transferCache?: {
            includeHeaders?: string[];
        } | boolean;
        timeout?: number;
    }): Observable<HttpResponse<ArrayBuffer>>;

7.  get(url: string, options: {
        headers?: HttpHeaders | Record<string, string | string[]>;
        observe: 'response';
        context?: HttpContext;
        params?: HttpParams | Record<string, string | number | boolean | ReadonlyArray<string | number | boolean>>;
        reportProgress?: boolean;
        responseType: 'blob';
        withCredentials?: boolean;
        credentials?: RequestCredentials;
        keepalive?: boolean;
        priority?: RequestPriority;
        cache?: RequestCache;
        mode?: RequestMode;
        redirect?: RequestRedirect;
        referrer?: string;
        integrity?: string;
        transferCache?: {
            includeHeaders?: string[];
        } | boolean;
        timeout?: number;
    }): Observable<HttpResponse<Blob>>;

// ... additional overloads for text, json response types with observe: 'response' are implied and would follow a similar pattern.

Parameters:
  url: The URL to request.
  options: Configuration options for the request.
    headers: Sets HTTP headers.
    observe: Specifies how to observe the response ('events' for progress events, 'response' for the full HttpResponse).
    context: Sets HttpContext for the request.
    params: Sets URL query parameters.
    reportProgress: If true, reports progress events.
    responseType: The type of the response body ('arraybuffer', 'blob', 'text', 'json').
    withCredentials: Whether to include credentials like cookies.
    credentials: Alias for withCredentials.
    keepalive: Indicates if the request should keep the connection alive.
    priority: Sets the priority of the request.
    cache: Configures caching behavior.
    mode: Sets the request mode (e.g., 'cors', 'no-cors').
    redirect: Configures redirect behavior.
    referrer: Sets the referrer header.
    integrity: Sets the Integrity header for SRI.
    transferCache: Configures transfer cache options.
    timeout: Sets a timeout for the request.

Returns:
  An Observable emitting HttpEvent or HttpResponse depending on the 'observe' option and the specified response type.
```

TITLE: TestBed Configuration and Utilities
DESCRIPTION: Provides methods for configuring the testing module, creating components, and managing the testing environment. Includes utilities for injecting dependencies and overriding module configurations.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/core/testing/index.api.md#_snippet_0

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
TestBed:
  // Static property providing access to the TestBed instance.
  static readonly TestBed: TestBedStatic;

  // Configures the compiler with specific options.
  configureCompiler(config: { providers?: any[]; useJit?: boolean }): void;
  // Configures the testing module with metadata.
  configureTestingModule(moduleDef: TestModuleMetadata): TestBed;
  // Creates a component instance within the testing module.
  createComponent<T>(component: Type<T>, options?: TestComponentOptions): ComponentFixture<T>;
  // Executes a function within the context of the testing module's injector.
  execute(tokens: any[], fn: Function, context?: any): any;
  // Initializes the testing environment with a root module and platform.
  initTestEnvironment(ngModule: Type<any> | Type<any>[], platform: PlatformRef, options?: TestEnvironmentOptions): void;
  // Injects a dependency token into a function.
  inject<T>(token: ProviderToken<T>, notFoundValue: undefined, options: InjectOptions & { optional?: false }): T;
  inject<T>(token: ProviderToken<T>, notFoundValue: null | undefined, options: InjectOptions): T | null;
  inject<T>(token: ProviderToken<T>, notFoundValue?: T, options?: InjectOptions): T;
  // Overrides the configuration of a component.
  overrideComponent(component: Type<any>, override: MetadataOverride<Component>): TestBed;
  // Overrides the configuration of a directive.
  overrideDirective(directive: Type<any>, override: MetadataOverride<Directive>): TestBed;
  // Overrides the configuration of an NgModule.
  overrideModule(ngModule: Type<any>, override: MetadataOverride<NgModule>): TestBed;
  // Overrides the configuration of a pipe.
  overridePipe(pipe: Type<any>, override: MetadataOverride<Pipe>): TestBed;
  // Overrides a provider with a new configuration.
  overrideProvider(token: any, provider: { useFactory: Function; deps: any[]; multi?: boolean }): TestBed;
  overrideProvider(token: any, provider: { useValue: any; multi?: boolean }): TestBed;
  overrideProvider(token: any, provider: { useFactory?: Function; useValue?: any; deps?: any[]; multi?: boolean }): TestBed;
  // Overrides the template of a component.
  overrideTemplate(component: Type<any>, template: string): TestBed;
  overrideTemplateUsingTestingModule(component: Type<any>, template: string): TestBed;
  // Resets the testing environment to its initial state.
  resetTestEnvironment(): void;
  // Resets the testing module, clearing configured components and providers.
  resetTestingModule(): TestBed;
  // Runs a function within an injection context.
  runInInjectionContext<T>(fn: () => T): T;
  // Deprecated: Flushes pending asynchronous operations related to effects.
  flushEffects(): void;
  // Gets the root NgModule of the testing environment.
  get ngModule(): Type<any> | Type<any>[];
  // Gets the PlatformRef of the testing environment.
  get platform(): PlatformRef;
```

TITLE: Angular Injector Methods
DESCRIPTION: Defines methods for interacting with Angular's dependency injection system, including retrieving tokens and running code within a specific context.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/core/index.api.md#_snippet_21

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Injector:
  abstract get<T>(token: string | ProviderToken<T>, notFoundValue?: any): T;
    - Retrieves an instance of a service or value associated with a given token.
    - Parameters:
      - token: The token (string or ProviderToken) to look up.
      - notFoundValue: Optional value to return if the token is not found.
    - Returns: The instance associated with the token, or notFoundValue if not found.

  abstract runInContext<ReturnT>(fn: () => ReturnT): ReturnT;
    - Executes a function within the injector's context, allowing access to its dependencies.
    - Parameters:
      - fn: The function to execute.
    - Returns: The return value of the executed function.
```

TITLE: HTTP Request Handling Patterns
DESCRIPTION: Illustrates common URI patterns handled by the in-memory web API service for emulating RESTful operations. It supports fetching all items, specific items by ID, and filtering using query parameters with regex support.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/packages/misc/angular-in-memory-web-api/README.md#_snippet_1

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
GET api/heroes          // Fetches all heroes from the 'heroes' collection.
GET api/heroes/42       // Fetches the hero with id=42 from the 'heroes' collection.
GET api/heroes?name=^j  // Fetches heroes whose name starts with 'j' or 'J' using a regex filter.
GET api/heroes.json/42  // Ignores the '.json' extension and fetches the hero with id=42.
```

Attribute:

  - Registers an early event contract for a specific application scope.

    - appId: A unique identifier for the application.
    - bubbleEventTypes: An array of event types that should bubble.
    - captureEventTypes: An array of event types that should capture.
    - dataContainer: Optional container for early event data.

  - Parameters:
    - appId: The unique identifier for the application.
    - dataContainer: Optional container for early event data.

EarlyJsactionDataContainer:
  - Interface for holding early event data, potentially keyed by application ID.
  - Properties:
    - _ejsa?: EarlyJsactionData: Data for a single application.
    - _ejsas?: { [appId: string]: EarlyJsactionData | undefined }: Data for multiple applications.

EventContract:
  - Manages event listeners and dispatching for a container.
  - constructor(containerManager: EventContractContainerManager)
  - Methods:
    - addEvent(eventType: string, prefixedEventType?: string, passive?: boolean): void
      - Adds an event listener for a specific event type.

      - Removes all registered event listeners.

      - Indicates support for special mouse event handling.

TITLE: Angular Animation Callbacks API
DESCRIPTION: References to browser APIs for handling animation and transition events. These callbacks allow developers to execute code when specific animation or transition states occur.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/guide/animations/migration.md#_snippet_16

LANGUAGE: apidoc
CODE:
```
Animation Event Callbacks:
  OnAnimationStart: Triggered when an animation starts.
  OnAnimationEnd: Triggered when an animation completes.
  OnAnimationIteration: Triggered after each iteration of an animation.
  OnAnimationCancel: Triggered when an animation is cancelled.

Transition Event Callbacks:
  OnTransitionStart: Triggered when a transition begins.
  OnTransitionRun: Triggered when a transition is about to occur.
  OnTransitionEnd: Triggered when a transition completes.
  OnTransitionCancel: Triggered when a transition is cancelled.

Note: Event bubbling can occur. Examine event properties like 'animationname' to identify the correct target.
```

TITLE: UrlSerializer API
DESCRIPTION: Defines the interface for serializing and parsing URL trees in Angular's router. It includes abstract methods for converting between URL strings and UrlTree objects.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/router/index.api.md#_snippet_46

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
abstract class UrlSerializer {
    // Parses a URL string into a UrlTree object.
    // @param url The URL string to parse.
    // @returns A UrlTree object representing the parsed URL.
    abstract parse(url: string): UrlTree;

    // Serializes a UrlTree object into a URL string.
    // @param tree The UrlTree object to serialize.
    // @returns A string representing the serialized URL.
    abstract serialize(tree: UrlTree): string;
}
```

TITLE: HarnessPredicate API Reference
DESCRIPTION: Provides details on the `HarnessPredicate` class and its methods for building complex filtering logic. It covers adding options, string matching, and how it integrates with `ComponentHarness` subclasses for targeted testing.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/guide/testing/creating-component-harnesses.md#_snippet_8

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
HarnessPredicate<T extends ComponentHarness>
  - A class used to define filtering criteria for `ComponentHarness` instances.

  Constructor(harnessType: HarnessConstructor<T>, options: object)
    - Initializes a new `HarnessPredicate`.
    - Parameters:
      - harnessType: The `ComponentHarness` subclass to create predicates for.
      - options: An object containing initial filter criteria.

  addOption(name: string, value: any, predicate: (harness: T, value: any) => Promise<boolean>): HarnessPredicate<T>
    - Adds a custom filter option to the predicate.
    - Parameters:
      - name: The name of the option (e.g., 'text', 'trigger text').
      - value: The value to filter by.
      - predicate: A function that takes the harness instance and the option value, returning a boolean indicating if the harness matches.
    - Returns: The `HarnessPredicate` instance for chaining.

  stringMatches(actual: string | null, expected: string | RegExp | null): boolean
    - A static helper method to compare strings, supporting exact matches or regular expressions.
    - Parameters:
      - actual: The actual string value from the harness.
      - expected: The expected string or RegExp to match against.
    - Returns: `true` if the strings match, `false` otherwise.

Usage:
  - Can be passed to `loader.getHarness()` or `locatorFor()` instead of a harness class.
  - Enables creating reusable and specific selectors for component instances.
  - Facilitates building powerful filtering APIs within harness classes.
```

TITLE: Angular HttpClient Configuration Mapping
DESCRIPTION: This documentation maps traditional `HttpClientModule`-based Angular configurations to their modern `provideHttpClient()` equivalents. It details how to migrate from NgModule providers to standalone API configuration functions, covering interceptors, JSONP, and XSRF protection.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/guide/http/setup.md#_snippet_10

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Angular HttpClient Configuration:

This table lists the NgModules available from `@angular/common/http` and how they relate to the provider configuration functions.

| **NgModule**                            | `provideHttpClient()` equivalent              |
|---------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------|
| `HttpClientModule`                      | `provideHttpClient(withInterceptorsFromDi())` |
| `HttpClientJsonpModule`                 | `withJsonpSupport()`                          |
| `HttpClientXsrfModule.withOptions(...)` | `withXsrfConfiguration(...)`                  |
| `HttpClientXsrfModule.disable()`        | `withNoXsrfProtection()`                      |

**Note on Multiple Injectors:**
Use caution when `HttpClientModule` is present in multiple injectors, as interceptor behavior can be poorly defined. Prefer `provideHttpClient` for multi-injector configurations due to its more stable behavior. See the `withRequestsMadeViaParent` feature for more details.
```

TITLE: Use `readonly` with Decorator-Based APIs
DESCRIPTION: When using decorator-based APIs like `@Output()` and query decorators (`@ViewChild`, `@ViewChildren`), apply the `readonly` modifier to the decorated properties. This reinforces that these properties are managed by Angular and should not be reassigned.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/best-practices/style-guide.md#_snippet_6

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
```
@Component({/* ... */})
export class UserProfile {
  @Output() readonly userSaved = new EventEmitter<void>();
  @ViewChildren(PaymentMethod) readonly paymentMethods?: QueryList<PaymentMethod>;
}
```

TITLE: Node.js: Patch Bluebird Promise with Zone.js
DESCRIPTION: Demonstrates how to patch Bluebird promises for zone awareness in a Node.js environment. This example shows how to apply the patch and run a Bluebird promise within a forked zone.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/packages/zone.js/NON-STANDARD-APIS.md#_snippet_4

LANGUAGE: javascript
CODE:
```
require('zone.js');
const Bluebird = require('bluebird');
require('zone.js/plugins/zone-bluebird');

const bluebirdSymbol = Zone.__symbol__('bluebird');
const patchBluebirdFn = (Zone as any)[bluebirdSymbol];
patchBluebirdFn(Bluebird);

Zone.current
  .fork({
    name: 'bluebird',
  })
  .run(() => {
    Bluebird.resolve(1).then((result) => {
      console.log('result ', result, 'Zone', Zone.current.name);
    });
  });
```

TITLE: Angular Async Validator Example
DESCRIPTION: This example demonstrates an Angular asynchronous validator function. It returns an Observable that emits either a ValidationErrors object if validation fails, or null if it succeeds, adhering to the AsyncValidatorFn API.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/reference/errors/NG01101.md#_snippet_0

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
```
import { AbstractControl, ValidationErrors } from '@angular/forms';
import { Observable, of } from 'rxjs';

export function isTenAsync(control: AbstractControl): 
  Observable<ValidationErrors | null> {
    const v: number = control.value;
    if (v !== 10) {
    // Emit an object with a validation error.
      return of({ 'notTen': true, 'requiredValue': 10 });
    }
    // Emit null, to indicate no error occurred.
    return of(null);
  }

```

TITLE: Angular WritableResource Interface
DESCRIPTION: Defines the WritableResource interface, which extends Resource and provides methods for managing a mutable resource. It includes methods to get a readonly version, check for a value, reload the resource, set a new value, and update the current value.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/core/index.api.md#_snippet_101

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
interface WritableResource<T> extends Resource<T> {
    // Returns a readonly version of the resource.
    asReadonly(): Resource<T>;
    
    // Checks if the resource currently holds a defined value.
    hasValue(): this is WritableResource<Exclude<T, undefined>>;
    
    // Reloads the resource from its source.
    reload(): boolean;
    
    // Sets the resource's value to a new value.
    set(value: T): void;
    
    // Updates the resource's value using an updater function.
    update(updater: (value: T) => T): void;
    
    // The current value of the resource, exposed as a writable signal.
    readonly value: WritableSignal<T>;
}
```

createCustomElement<P>(component: Type<any>, config: NgElementConfig): NgElementConstructor<P>
  - Creates a custom element constructor from an Angular component.
  - Parameters:
    - component: The Angular component Type to convert.
    - config: Configuration object for the custom element.

NgElement
  - Abstract base class for custom elements created by @angular/elements.
  - Methods:
    - attributeChangedCallback(attrName: string, oldValue: string | null, newValue: string, namespace?: string): void
      - Called when an observed attribute has been added, removed, updated, or replaced.
    - connectedCallback(): void
      - Called when the element is first connected to the document's DOM.
    - disconnectedCallback(): void
      - Called when the element is disconnected from the document's DOM.
  - Properties:
    - ngElementEventsSubscription: Subscription | null
      - Subscription to events from the element's strategy.
    - ngElementStrategy: NgElementStrategy
      - The strategy used by the element to handle inputs, outputs, and lifecycle.

NgElementConfig
  - Configuration options for creating a custom element.
  - Properties:
    - injector: Injector
      - The Angular Injector to use for creating the component.
    - strategyFactory?: NgElementStrategyFactory
      - An optional factory to create the element's strategy.

NgElementConstructor<P>
  - Represents the constructor for a custom element created by @angular/elements.
  - Properties:
    - observedAttributes: string[]
      - A static list of attribute names that the custom element should observe.
  - Methods:
    - new (injector?: Injector): NgElement & WithProperties<P>
      - Creates a new instance of the custom element.

NgElementStrategy
  - Interface for the strategy that manages the lifecycle and I/O of a custom element.
  - Methods:
    - connect(element: HTMLElement): void
      - Connects the strategy to the host element.
    - disconnect(): void
      - Disconnects the strategy from the host element.
    - events: Observable<NgElementStrategyEvent>
      - An observable stream of events emitted by the strategy.
    - getInputValue(propName: string): any
      - Retrieves the current value of an input property.
    - setInputValue(propName: string, value: string, transform?: (value: any) => any): void
      - Sets the value of an input property, optionally applying a transformation.

NgElementStrategyEvent
  - Represents an event emitted by an NgElementStrategy.
  - Properties:
    - name: string
      - The name of the event.
    - value: any
      - The payload of the event.

NgElementStrategyFactory
  - Factory interface for creating NgElementStrategy instances.
  - Methods:
    - create(injector: Injector): NgElementStrategy
      - Creates and returns a new NgElementStrategy.

VERSION: Version
  - The version of the @angular/elements package.

WithProperties<P>
  - Utility type to add properties of type P to an object.
  - Type Parameters:
    - P: The type whose properties are to be added.
  - Usage:
    - { [property in keyof P]: P[property] }
```

TITLE: HttpClient GET Method Overloads
DESCRIPTION: Details the various overloads for the `HttpClient.get` method, allowing for different response types (Blob, text, JSON, generic T) and observation modes ('response' or 'body'). It covers common options like headers, context, parameters, and progress reporting.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/common/http/index.api.md#_snippet_7

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
HttpClient.get

Provides methods for making HTTP GET requests.

Overloads:

1.  `get(url: string, options: { observe: 'response'; responseType: 'blob'; ... }): Observable<HttpResponse<Blob>>`
    - Fetches data as a Blob.
    - `observe`: Must be 'response' to get the full HttpResponse.
    - `responseType`: Specifies 'blob' for binary data.

2.  `get(url: string, options: { observe: 'response'; responseType: 'text'; ... }): Observable<HttpResponse<string>>`
    - Fetches data as plain text.
    - `observe`: Must be 'response'.
    - `responseType`: Specifies 'text' for string data.

3.  `get(url: string, options: { observe: 'response'; responseType?: 'json'; ... }): Observable<HttpResponse<Object>>`
    - Fetches data as a JSON object (untyped).
    - `observe`: Must be 'response'.
    - `responseType`: Defaults to 'json' if not specified, returning an untyped Object.

4.  `get<T>(url: string, options: { observe: 'response'; responseType?: 'json'; ... }): Observable<HttpResponse<T>>`
    - Fetches data as a JSON object with a specific type `T`.
    - `observe`: Must be 'response'.
    - `responseType`: Defaults to 'json', returning a typed object.

5.  `get(url: string, options?: { observe?: 'body'; responseType?: 'json'; ... }): Observable<Object>`
    - Fetches the response body as a JSON object (untyped).
    - `observe`: Defaults to 'body' if not specified, returning only the body.
    - `responseType`: Defaults to 'json'.

6.  `get<T>(url: string, options?: { observe?: 'body'; responseType?: 'json'; ... }): Observable<T>`
    - Fetches the response body as a JSON object with a specific type `T`.
    - `observe`: Defaults to 'body'.
    - `responseType`: Defaults to 'json'.

Common Options:
- `headers`: HttpHeaders or Record<string, string | string[]> for request headers.
- `context`: HttpContext for request context.
- `params`: HttpParams or Record for URL query parameters.
- `reportProgress`: boolean to enable progress reporting.
- `withCredentials`: boolean to include credentials.
- `timeout`: number for request timeout in milliseconds.
- `transferCache`: object or boolean to configure transfer cache.

Returns: An Observable emitting the HttpResponse or the response body, depending on the `observe` option.
```

TITLE: Angular Injector Class API
DESCRIPTION: Defines the abstract Injector class, its static methods for creating injectors, and the abstract method for retrieving dependencies. Includes deprecated methods and static properties.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/core/index.api.md#_snippet_32

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Injector:
  abstract class Injector
    // Static methods
    static create(providers: StaticProvider[], parent?: Injector): Injector
      - Creates an Injector with a list of providers and an optional parent Injector.
      - @deprecated (undocumented)

    static create(options: { providers: Array<Provider | StaticProvider>, parent?: Injector, name?: string }): DestroyableInjector
      - Creates an Injector with configuration options including providers, parent, and name.

    static NULL: Injector
      - A null Injector that does not provide any dependencies.

    static THROW_IF_NOT_FOUND: {}
      - A sentinel value used to indicate that a dependency should not be found.

    // Abstract methods
    abstract get<T>(token: ProviderToken<T>, notFoundValue: undefined, options: InjectOptions & { optional?: false }): T
      - Retrieves a dependency by its token. Throws an error if not found and notOptional is true.
      - Parameters:
        - token: The token of the dependency to retrieve.
        - notFoundValue: Undefined, indicating an error should be thrown if not found.
        - options: InjectOptions specifying retrieval behavior (e.g., optional).
      - Returns: The requested dependency instance.

    abstract get<T>(token: ProviderToken<T>, notFoundValue: null | undefined, options: InjectOptions): T | null
      - Retrieves a dependency by its token. Returns null or undefined if not found based on notFoundValue.
      - Parameters:
        - token: The token of the dependency to retrieve.
        - notFoundValue: Null or undefined, indicating a fallback value if not found.
        - options: InjectOptions specifying retrieval behavior.
      - Returns: The requested dependency instance or the fallback value.

    abstract get<T>(token: ProviderToken<T>, notFoundValue?: T, options?: InjectOptions): T
      - Generic method to retrieve a dependency by its token with an optional fallback value and options.
      - Parameters:
        - token: The token of the dependency to retrieve.
        - notFoundValue: An optional fallback value if the dependency is not found.
        - options: Optional InjectOptions.
      - Returns: The requested dependency instance or the fallback value.

    abstract get<T>(token: string | ProviderToken<T>, notFoundValue?: any): any
      - @deprecated (undocumented) - Legacy method signature.

    // Internal properties
    readonly ɵprov: unknown
      - Internal property for provider information.

```

TITLE: Angular Rendering API
DESCRIPTION: Defines the core abstract classes and interfaces for Angular's rendering engine. `Renderer2` provides methods for DOM manipulation, `RendererFactory2` creates `Renderer2` instances, and related types define renderer capabilities and style flags.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/core/index.api.md#_snippet_80

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
export abstract class Renderer2 {
    abstract addClass(el: any, name: string): void;
    abstract appendChild(parent: any, newChild: any): void;
    abstract createComment(value: string): any;
    abstract createElement(name: string, namespace?: string | null): any;
    abstract createText(value: string): any;
    abstract get data(): { [key: string]: any };
    abstract destroy(): void;
    destroyNode: ((node: any) => void) | null;
    abstract insertBefore(parent: any, newChild: any, refChild: any, isMove?: boolean): void;
    abstract listen(target: 'window' | 'document' | 'body' | any, eventName: string, callback: (event: any) => boolean | void, options?: ListenerOptions): () => void;
    abstract nextSibling(node: any): any;
    abstract parentNode(node: any): any;
    abstract removeAttribute(el: any, name: string, namespace?: string | null): void;
    abstract removeChild(parent: any, oldChild: any, isHostElement?: boolean): void;
    abstract removeClass(el: any, name: string): void;
    abstract removeStyle(el: any, style: string, flags?: RendererStyleFlags2): void;
    abstract selectRootElement(selectorOrNode: string | any, preserveContent?: boolean): any;
    abstract setAttribute(el: any, name: string, value: string, namespace?: string | null): void;
    abstract setProperty(el: any, name: string, value: any): void;
    abstract setStyle(el: any, style: string, value: any, flags?: RendererStyleFlags2): void;
    abstract setValue(node: any, value: string): void;
}
  - Abstract base class for rendering operations.
  - Provides methods for DOM manipulation like adding/removing classes, setting attributes, creating elements, listening to events, etc.
  - Implementations vary based on the rendering target (e.g., browser DOM, server-side rendering).

export abstract class RendererFactory2 {
    abstract begin?(): void;
    abstract createRenderer(hostElement: any, type: RendererType2 | null): Renderer2;
    abstract end?(): void;
    abstract whenRenderingDone?(): Promise<any>;
}
  - Factory for creating `Renderer2` instances.
  - `createRenderer`: Creates a `Renderer2` instance for a given host element and renderer type.
  - `begin`/`end`: Optional methods for managing rendering phases.
  - `whenRenderingDone`: An optional promise that resolves when rendering is complete.

export enum RendererStyleFlags2 {
    DashCase = 2,
    Important = 1
}
  - Flags used with style manipulation methods in `Renderer2`.
  - `DashCase`: Indicates style properties are in dash-case (e.g., 'background-color').
  - `Important`: Indicates the style should be applied with `!important`.

export interface RendererType2 {
    data: { [kind: string]: any };
    encapsulation: ViewEncapsulation;
}
  - Provides metadata about the renderer, such as encapsulation mode and custom data.
```

TITLE: Testing httpResource with HttpClientTestingController
DESCRIPTION: Provides an example of unit testing code that uses httpResource. It demonstrates setting up the testing module, injecting necessary services, triggering requests, and flushing mock responses using HttpTestingController.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/guide/http/http-resource.md#_snippet_5

LANGUAGE: ts
CODE:
```
TestBed.configureTestingModule({
  providers: [
    provideHttpClient(),
    provideHttpClientTesting(),
  ],
});

const id = signal(0);
const mockBackend = TestBed.inject(HttpTestingController);
const response = httpResource(() => `/data/${id()}`, {injector: TestBed.inject(Injector)});
TestBed.tick(); // Triggers the effect
const firstRequest = mockBackend.expectOne('/data/0');
firstRequest.flush(0);

// Ensures the values are propagated to the httpResource
await TestBed.inject(ApplicationRef).whenStable();

expect(response.value()).toEqual(0);
```

TITLE: Angular SSR API Documentation
DESCRIPTION: Provides details on key APIs for configuring server-side rendering (SSR) and hybrid rendering strategies in Angular. This includes route configuration, rendering modes, and provider functions.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/guide/ssr.md#_snippet_5

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
ServerRoute:
  Represents a route configuration for server-side rendering.
  Properties:
    path: string - The route path (e.g., '', '/about').
    renderMode: RenderMode - The rendering mode for this route.

RenderMode:
  Enum defining the rendering strategy for a route.
  Members:
    Server: Renders the application on the server for each request (SSR).
    Client: Renders the application in the browser (CSR), the default Angular behavior.
    Prerender: Prerenders the application at build time, generating static HTML files (SSG).

provideServerRendering(options?: ServerRenderingOptions):
  Provides the server rendering providers for an Angular application.
  Options:
    routes?: ServerRoute[] - An array of ServerRoute objects to configure routing.
    appShell?: Type<any> - The component to use as the app shell for CSR routes.

withRoutes(routes: ServerRoute[]):
  A function that configures server routes for `provideServerRendering`.

withAppShell(appShellComponent: Type<any>):
  A function that configures an app shell component for `provideServerRendering`.

outputMode:
  Configuration option to control the build output.
  Values:
    static: Generates a fully static application.
    ssr: Enables server-side rendering.

Server routing:
  Configuring server routes involves declaring an array of `ServerRoute` objects, typically in `app.routes.server.ts`.
  This configuration is then passed to `provideServerRendering` using `withRoutes`.

App shell pattern:
  When using the App shell pattern, specify the component for client-side rendered routes using `withAppShell`.
```

TITLE: Angular Tutorial Directory Structure
DESCRIPTION: Details the expected file and directory organization for Angular embedded tutorials, including introduction, steps, and the common project structure.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/tutorials/README.md#_snippet_1

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Tutorial Directory Structure:
  - Introduction:
    - Path: src/content/tutorials/<tutorial-name>/intro
    - Route: /tutorials/<tutorial-name>
    - Contains: README.md (content), config.json (configuration), source code
  - Steps:
    - Path: src/content/tutorials/<tutorial-name>/steps/<step-number>-<step-pathname>
    - Route: /tutorials/<tutorial-name>/<step-pathname>
    - Step Numbering: Defines order, e.g., '1-components-in-angular'
  - Common Project:
    - Path: src/content/tutorials/common
    - Contains: package.json, tsconfig.json, angular.json, main.ts, app.module.ts, etc.
    - Reused by all tutorials for dependencies and project setup.
  - Reserved Directories:
    - playground: Source code for the /playground route.
    - homepage: Source code for the homepage playground.
```

TITLE: In-Memory Web API Commands
DESCRIPTION: Describes client commands to interact with the in-memory web API service for state management. Covers resetting the database and getting/updating service configuration.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/packages/misc/angular-in-memory-web-api/README.md#_snippet_7

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
In-Memory Web API Commands:

When the last segment of the _api base path_ is ""commands"", the `collectionName` is treated as the _command_.

Example URLs:
  commands/resetdb   // Reset the ""database"" to its original state
  commands/config    // Get or update this service's config object

Usage:
  http.post('commands/resetdb', undefined);
  http.get('commands/config');
  http.post('commands/config', '{""delay"":1000}');

Command requests do not simulate real remote data access; they respond as quickly as possible.

The `resetDb` command calls your `InMemoryDbService` data service's [`createDb` method](#createDb) with the `RequestInfo` object, enabling the `createDb` logic to adjust its behavior per the client request.

Example with reset option:
```ts
http
  // Reset the database collections with the `clear` option
  .post('commands/resetDb', { clear: true })

  // when command finishes, get heroes
  .concatMap(
    ()=> http.get<Data>('api/heroes')
        .map(data => data.data as Hero[])
  )

  // execute the request sequence and
  // do something with the heroes
  .subscribe(...)
```
```

TITLE: TestBed Static Methods
DESCRIPTION: Documentation for the primary static methods of the Angular TestBed class, used for configuring and managing the testing environment. These methods are typically called within beforeEach blocks for isolated test execution.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/guide/testing/utility-apis.md#_snippet_8

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
TestBed Static Methods:

configureTestingModule(metadata: TestModuleMetadata)
  - Configures the testing module with the provided metadata. This allows customization of imports, declarations, and providers for tests.
  - Parameters:
    - metadata: An object conforming to TestModuleMetadata, specifying the testing module's configuration.
  - Details: Call this within a beforeEach() block to set up the testing module for each test. The testing shims establish an initial environment, and this method refines it.

compileComponents()
  - Asynchronously compiles the components, directives, and pipes declared in the testing module. This is mandatory if any components use templateUrl or styleUrls.
  - Returns: A Promise that resolves when compilation is complete.
  - Details: Must be called after configureTestingModule and before creating components. Once called, the TestBed configuration is frozen for the current spec.

createComponent<T>(component: Type<T>): ComponentFixture<T>
  - Creates an instance of a component of type T based on the current TestBed configuration.
  - Parameters:
    - component: The component class to instantiate.
  - Returns: A ComponentFixture<T> object, providing access to the component instance, its debug element, and other testing utilities.
  - Details: After calling createComponent, the TestBed configuration is frozen for the duration of the current spec.

overrideModule(moduleType: Type<any>, override: MetadataOverride<NgModule>)
  - Replaces or modifies metadata for a given NgModule within the testing module configuration.
  - Parameters:
    - moduleType: The NgModule class whose metadata needs to be overridden.
    - override: An object conforming to MetadataOverride<NgModule> specifying the changes (add, remove, set).
  - Details: This method can modify nested modules imported by the current testing module, allowing deep customization of the testing environment.
```

TITLE: Angular ViewRef API
DESCRIPTION: Defines the ViewRef API, an abstract class that serves as the base for all views in Angular. It provides methods for destroying the view and checking its destroyed state, and for registering destruction callbacks.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/core/index.api.md#_snippet_100

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
abstract class ViewRef extends ChangeDetectorRef {
    // Destroys the view and its associated components.
    abstract destroy(): void;
    
    // Checks if the view has been destroyed.
    abstract get destroyed(): boolean;
    
    // Registers a callback function to be executed when the view is destroyed.
    abstract onDestroy(callback: Function): void;
}

TITLE: PathLocationStrategy API
DESCRIPTION: Implements LocationStrategy and provides methods for interacting with the browser's history API. It handles URL manipulation, navigation events, and state management for client-side routing.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/common/index.api.md#_snippet_33

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
class PathLocationStrategy extends LocationStrategy implements OnDestroy {
    constructor(_platformLocation: PlatformLocation, href?: string);

    // Navigates back in the browser history.
    back(): void;

    // Navigates forward in the browser history.
    forward(): void;

    // Retrieves the base href of the application.
    getBaseHref(): string;

    // Retrieves the current state object associated with the history entry.
    getState(): unknown;

    // Navigates to a specific point in the browser history.
    // relativePosition: The position relative to the current history entry (e.g., -1 for previous, 1 for next).
    historyGo(relativePosition?: number): void;

    // Lifecycle hook called when the component is destroyed.
    ngOnDestroy(): void;

    // Registers a listener for popstate events (e.g., when the user navigates using back/forward buttons).
    // fn: The callback function to execute when a popstate event occurs.
    onPopState(fn: LocationChangeListener): void;

    // Returns the current URL path, optionally including the hash.
    // includeHash: If true, includes the hash part of the URL.
    path(includeHash?: boolean): string;

    // Prepares an internal URL for external use, ensuring it's correctly formatted.
    // internal: The internal URL path to prepare.
    prepareExternalUrl(internal: string): string;

    // Pushes a new history entry onto the browser's history stack.
    // state: The state object to associate with the new history entry.
    // title: The title for the new history entry.
    // url: The URL for the new history entry.
    // queryParams: Query parameters to append to the URL.
    pushState(state: any, title: string, url: string, queryParams: string): void;

    // Replaces the current history entry with a new one.
    // state: The state object for the replacement.
    // title: The title for the replacement.
    // url: The URL for the replacement.
    // queryParams: Query parameters to append to the URL.
    replaceState(state: any, title: string, url: string, queryParams: string): void;

    static ɵfac: i0.ɵɵFactoryDeclaration<PathLocationStrategy, [null, { optional: true }]>;
    static ɵprov: i0.ɵɵInjectableDeclaration<PathLocationStrategy>;
}
```

TITLE: LocationStrategy API
DESCRIPTION: Defines the API for location strategies in Angular, abstracting browser history and URL manipulation. It includes methods for navigation, state management, and URL preparation.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/common/index.api.md#_snippet_15

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
LocationStrategy API:
  Abstract class defining the interface for location strategies.

  Methods:
    abstract back(): void
      Navigates to the previous location in the browser history.

    abstract forward(): void
      Navigates to the next location in the browser history.

    abstract getBaseHref(): string
      Returns the base URL of the application.

    abstract getState(): unknown
      Retrieves the current state object associated with the location.

    historyGo?(relativePosition: number): void
      Navigates to a specific location in the browser history relative to the current position.
      (Optional method, may not be implemented by all strategies).

    abstract onPopState(fn: LocationChangeListener): void
      Subscribes to browser history events (e.g., back/forward button clicks).
      The provided function `fn` will be called with a LocationChangeEvent.

    abstract path(includeHash?: boolean): string
      Returns the current URL path.
      `includeHash`: If true, includes the URL hash fragment.

    abstract prepareExternalUrl(internal: string): string
      Converts an internal application URL into an absolute URL.

    abstract pushState(state: any, title: string, url: string, queryParams: string): void
      Pushes a new history entry onto the browser's history stack.
      `state`: An object representing the history state.
      `title`: The title for the new history entry.
      `url`: The URL for the new history entry.
      `queryParams`: The query parameters for the new history entry.

    abstract replaceState(state: any, title: string, url: string, queryParams: string): void
      Replaces the current history entry with a new one.
      `state`: An object representing the history state.
      `title`: The title for the new history entry.
      `url`: The URL for the new history entry.
      `queryParams`: The query parameters for the new history entry.

  Static Properties:
    static ɵfac: i0.ɵɵFactoryDeclaration<LocationStrategy, never>
    static ɵprov: i0.ɵɵInjectableDeclaration<LocationStrategy>
```

TITLE: Angular HttpRequest Class API
DESCRIPTION: Provides a comprehensive overview of the HttpRequest class, including its constructors for creating requests with various methods and bodies, its properties for accessing request details, and utility methods like clone for request modification.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/common/http/index.api.md#_snippet_39

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
HttpRequest<T>

Represents an outgoing request, which can be observed for progress events.

Constructors:

  constructor(method: 'GET' | 'HEAD' | 'DELETE', url: string, init?: { headers?: HttpHeaders; context?: HttpContext; reportProgress?: boolean; params?: HttpParams; responseType?: 'arraybuffer' | 'blob' | 'json' | 'text'; withCredentials?: boolean; credentials?: RequestCredentials; keepalive?: boolean; priority?: RequestPriority; cache?: RequestCache; mode?: RequestMode; redirect?: RequestRedirect; referrer?: string; integrity?: string; timeout?: number; })
    - Initializes a new HttpRequest instance for GET, HEAD, or DELETE methods.
    - Parameters:
      - method: The HTTP method ('GET', 'HEAD', or 'DELETE').
      - url: The URL for the request.
      - init: Optional configuration object for the request.

  constructor(method: 'POST', url: string, body: T | null, init?: { headers?: HttpHeaders; context?: HttpContext; reportProgress?: boolean; params?: HttpParams; responseType?: 'arraybuffer' | 'blob' | 'json' | 'text'; withCredentials?: boolean; credentials?: RequestCredentials; keepalive?: boolean; priority?: RequestPriority; cache?: RequestCache; mode?: RequestMode; redirect?: RequestRedirect; referrer?: string; integrity?: string; transferCache?: { includeHeaders?: string[]; } | boolean; timeout?: number; })
    - Initializes a new HttpRequest instance for POST requests, allowing a request body.
    - Parameters:
      - method: The HTTP method ('POST').
      - url: The URL for the request.
      - body: The request body, which can be of any type T or null.
      - init: Optional configuration object for the request, including transferCache.

  constructor(method: 'PUT' | 'PATCH', url: string, body: T | null, init?: { headers?: HttpHeaders; context?: HttpContext; reportProgress?: boolean; params?: HttpParams; responseType?: 'arraybuffer' | 'blob' | 'json' | 'text'; withCredentials?: boolean; credentials?: RequestCredentials; keepalive?: boolean; priority?: RequestPriority; cache?: RequestCache; timeout?: number; mode?: RequestMode; redirect?: RequestRedirect; referrer?: string; integrity?: string; })
    - Initializes a new HttpRequest instance for PUT or PATCH requests, allowing a request body.
    - Parameters:
      - method: The HTTP method ('PUT' or 'PATCH').
      - url: The URL for the request.
      - body: The request body, which can be of any type T or null.
      - init: Optional configuration object for the request.

  constructor(method: string, url: string, body: T | null, init?: { headers?: HttpHeaders; context?: HttpContext; reportProgress?: boolean; params?: HttpParams; responseType?: 'arraybuffer' | 'blob' | 'json' | 'text'; withCredentials?: boolean; credentials?: RequestCredentials; keepalive?: boolean; priority?: RequestPriority; cache?: RequestCache; mode?: RequestMode; redirect?: RequestRedirect; referrer?: string; integrity?: string; transferCache?: { includeHeaders?: string[]; } | boolean; timeout?: number; })
    - A general constructor for any HTTP method, allowing a request body and comprehensive initialization options.
    - Parameters:
      - method: The HTTP method (e.g., 'GET', 'POST', 'PUT', 'DELETE', 'PATCH', 'OPTIONS', etc.).
      - url: The URL for the request.
      - body: The request body, which can be of any type T or null.
      - init: Optional configuration object for the request.

Properties:

  readonly body: T | null;
    - The request body.

  readonly cache: RequestCache;
    - The cache configuration for the request.

  readonly context: HttpContext;
    - The HttpContext associated with the request.

  readonly credentials: RequestCredentials;
    - The credentials to use for the request.

  readonly headers: HttpHeaders;
    - The HTTP headers for the request.

  readonly integrity: string;
    - The Subresource Integrity value for the request.

  readonly keepalive: boolean;
    - Indicates if the request should use the keepalive mechanism.

  readonly method: string;
    - The HTTP method of the request.

  readonly mode: RequestMode;
    - The mode for the request (e.g., 'cors', 'no-cors').

  readonly params: HttpParams;
    - The HTTP parameters for the request.

  readonly priority: RequestPriority;
    - The priority of the request.

  readonly redirect: RequestRedirect;
    - The redirect mode for the request (e.g., 'follow', 'error').

  readonly referrer: string;
    - The referrer policy for the request.

  readonly reportProgress: boolean;
    - Indicates if progress events should be reported.

  readonly responseType: 'arraybuffer' | 'blob' | 'json' | 'text';
    - The expected response type.

  readonly timeout?: number;
    - The timeout duration for the request.

  readonly transferCache?: { includeHeaders?: string[]; } | boolean;
    - Configuration for transfer cache.

Methods:

  clone(update?: { headers?: HttpHeaders; context?: HttpContext; reportProgress?: boolean; params?: HttpParams; responseType?: 'arraybuffer' | 'blob' | 'json' | 'text'; withCredentials?: boolean; credentials?: RequestCredentials; keepalive?: boolean; priority?: RequestPriority; cache?: RequestCache; mode?: RequestMode; redirect?: RequestRedirect; referrer?: string; integrity?: string; transferCache?: { includeHeaders?: string[]; } | boolean; timeout?: number; body?: T | null; method?: string; url?: string; setHeaders?: { [name: string]: string | string[]; }; setParams?: { [param: string]: string; }; }): HttpRequest<T>;
    - Creates a new HttpRequest instance with the provided updates.
    - Parameters:
      - update: An object containing properties to update in the new HttpRequest.
    - Returns: A new HttpRequest instance.

  clone<V>(update: { headers?: HttpHeaders; context?: HttpContext; reportProgress?: boolean; params?: HttpParams; responseType?: 'arraybuffer' | 'blob' | 'json' | 'text'; keepalive?: boolean; priority?: RequestPriority; cache?: RequestCache; mode?: RequestMode; redirect?: RequestRedirect; referrer?: string; integrity?: string; withCredentials?: boolean; credentials?: RequestCredentials; transferCache?: { includeHeaders?: string[]; } | boolean; timeout?: number; body?: V | null; method?: string; url?: string; setHeaders?: { [name: string]: string | string[]; }; setParams?: { [param: string]: string; }; }): HttpRequest<V>;
    - Creates a new HttpRequest instance with the provided updates and a potentially different body type.
    - Parameters:
      - update: An object containing properties to update in the new HttpRequest.
    - Returns: A new HttpRequest instance with the specified generic type V.

  detectContentTypeHeader(): string | null;
    - Detects the Content-Type header based on the request body.
    - Returns: The detected Content-Type header string or null.

  serializeBody(): ArrayBuffer | Blob | FormData | URLSearchParams | string | null;
    - Serializes the request body into a format suitable for sending.
    - Returns: The serialized request body or null.
```

TITLE: ContentChildren Decorator and Function

CODE:
```
ContentChildren Decorator:
  (selector: ProviderToken<unknown> | Function | string, opts?: { descendants?: boolean; emitDistinctChangesOnly?: boolean; read?: any; }): any;
  new (selector: ProviderToken<unknown> | Function | string, opts?: { descendants?: boolean; emitDistinctChangesOnly?: boolean; read?: any; }): Query;

ContentChildren Function:
  <LocatorT>(locator: ProviderToken<LocatorT> | string, opts?: { descendants?: boolean; read?: undefined; debugName?: string; }): Signal<ReadonlyArray<LocatorT>>;
  <LocatorT, ReadT>(locator: ProviderToken<LocatorT> | string, opts: { descendants?: boolean; read: ProviderToken<ReadT>; debugName?: string; }): Signal<ReadonlyArray<ReadT>>;

Parameters:

TITLE: Angular Animations API Reference
DESCRIPTION: Comprehensive documentation for Angular's animation system. This includes functions for defining animation states, sequences, transitions, and triggers, as well as the NoopAnimationPlayer class for managing animation playback. It covers the core building blocks for creating complex animations within Angular applications.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/animations/index.api.md#_snippet_1

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Angular Animations API:

// Interfaces
export interface AnimationTriggerMetadata extends AnimationMetadata {
    definitions: AnimationMetadata[];
    name: string;
    options: { params?: { [name: string]: any; } } | null;
}

// Constants
export const AUTO_STYLE = ""*"";

// Functions
export function group(steps: AnimationMetadata[], options?: AnimationOptions | null): AnimationGroupMetadata;
  // Creates a parallel animation group.
  // Parameters:
  //   steps: An array of AnimationMetadata objects to be played in parallel.
  //   options: Optional configuration for the group.
  // Returns: An AnimationGroupMetadata object.

export function keyframes(steps: AnimationStyleMetadata[]): AnimationKeyframesSequenceMetadata;
  // Creates a keyframe sequence animation.
  // Parameters:
  //   steps: An array of AnimationStyleMetadata objects defining keyframes.
  // Returns: An AnimationKeyframesSequenceMetadata object.

export function query(selector: string, animation: AnimationMetadata | AnimationMetadata[], options?: AnimationQueryOptions | null): AnimationQueryMetadata;
  // Queries for elements within the animation tree and applies animations to them.
  // Parameters:
  //   selector: A CSS selector to find elements.
  //   animation: The animation to apply to the selected elements.
  //   options: Optional configuration for the query.
  // Returns: An AnimationQueryMetadata object.

export function sequence(steps: AnimationMetadata[], options?: AnimationOptions | null): AnimationSequenceMetadata;
  // Creates a sequential animation sequence.
  // Parameters:
  //   steps: An array of AnimationMetadata objects to be played in sequence.
  //   options: Optional configuration for the sequence.
  // Returns: An AnimationSequenceMetadata object.

export function stagger(timings: string | number, animation: AnimationMetadata | AnimationMetadata[]): AnimationStaggerMetadata;
  // Applies a stagger effect to a collection of animations.
  // Parameters:
  //   timings: The timing for the stagger effect (e.g., '50ms 100ms').
  //   animation: The animation to apply the stagger effect to.
  // Returns: An AnimationStaggerMetadata object.

export function state(name: string, styles: AnimationStyleMetadata, options?: { params: { [name: string]: any; }; }): AnimationStateMetadata;
  // Defines a named animation state.
  // Parameters:
  //   name: The name of the state.
  //   styles: The styles associated with this state.
  //   options: Optional parameters for the state.
  // Returns: An AnimationStateMetadata object.

export function style(tokens: '*' | { [key: string]: string | number; } | Array<'*' | { [key: string]: string | number; }>): AnimationStyleMetadata;
  // Defines a set of CSS styles for an animation step.
  // Parameters:
  //   tokens: A style object or an array of style objects.
  // Returns: An AnimationStyleMetadata object.

export function transition(stateChangeExpr: string | ((fromState: string, toState: string, element?: any, params?: { [key: string]: any; }) => boolean), steps: AnimationMetadata | AnimationMetadata[], options?: AnimationOptions | null): AnimationTransitionMetadata;
  // Defines a transition between animation states.
  // Parameters:
  //   stateChangeExpr: A string or function defining the state change.
  //   steps: The animation steps to execute during the transition.
  //   options: Optional configuration for the transition.
  // Returns: An AnimationTransitionMetadata object.

export function trigger(name: string, definitions: AnimationMetadata[]): AnimationTriggerMetadata;
  // Defines an animation trigger that can be attached to an element.
  // Parameters:
  //   name: The name of the trigger.
  //   definitions: An array of animation metadata (states, transitions) for the trigger.
  // Returns: An AnimationTriggerMetadata object.

export function useAnimation(animation: AnimationReferenceMetadata, options?: AnimationOptions | null): AnimationAnimateRefMetadata;
  // Reuses a previously defined animation.
  // Parameters:
  //   animation: A reference to the animation to reuse.
  //   options: Optional configuration for reusing the animation.
  // Returns: An AnimationAnimateRefMetadata object.

// Classes
export class NoopAnimationPlayer implements AnimationPlayer {
    constructor(duration?: number, delay?: number);
      // Initializes the player.
      init(): void;
      // Starts the animation playback.
      play(): void;
      // Pauses the animation.
      pause(): void;
      // Restarts the animation from the beginning.
      restart(): void;
      // Stops and cleans up the animation.
      destroy(): void;
      // Finishes the animation immediately.
      finish(): void;
      // Resets the animation to its initial state.
      reset(): void;
      // Sets the current playback position.
      setPosition(position: number): void;
      // Gets the current playback position.
      getPosition(): number;
      // Checks if the animation has started.
      hasStarted(): boolean;
      // Registers a callback for when the animation is destroyed.
      onDestroy(fn: () => void): void;
      // Registers a callback for when the animation completes.
      onDone(fn: () => void): void;
      // Registers a callback for when the animation starts.
      onStart(fn: () => void): void;
      // Reference to the parent player if nested.
      parentPlayer: AnimationPlayer | null;
      // The total duration of the animation.
      readonly totalTime: number;
}

```

TITLE: HttpClient Request Body Serialization
DESCRIPTION: Explains how HttpClient serializes different types of data provided as the request body for POST or PUT requests. Covers serialization to plain text, JSON, and multipart/form-data.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/guide/http/making-requests.md#_snippet_4

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
HttpClient.post(url: string, body: any, options?: any): Observable<...>

// Parameter: body
// Type: any
// Description: The data to send in the request body. HttpClient serializes the body based on its type:
//   - string: Serialized as plain text.
//   - number, boolean, array, or plain object: Serialized as JSON.
//   - ArrayBuffer: Sent as raw data from the buffer.
//   - Blob: Sent as raw data with the Blob's content type.
//   - FormData: Encoded as `multipart/form-data`.
//   - HttpParams or URLSearchParams: Formatted as `application/x-www-form-urlencoded` string.

// Example Usage:
// http.post('/submit', 'plain text data')
// http.post('/save', { name: 'item', value: 10 })
// http.post('/upload', formData)

// Important: Remember to subscribe to the Observable returned by mutation requests (like POST) to ensure the request is actually sent.
```

TITLE: ContentChild Decorator and Function
DESCRIPTION: APIs for querying and injecting a single content child element or directive within a component's template. Supports various selectors and options for descendants and read types.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/core/index.api.md#_snippet_5

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
ContentChild Decorator:
  (selector: ProviderToken<unknown> | Function | string, opts?: { descendants?: boolean; read?: any; static?: boolean; }): any;
  new (selector: ProviderToken<unknown> | Function | string, opts?: { descendants?: boolean; read?: any; static?: boolean; }): ContentChild;

ContentChild Function:
  <LocatorT>(locator: ProviderToken<LocatorT> | string, opts?: { descendants?: boolean; read?: undefined; debugName?: string; }): Signal<LocatorT | undefined>;
  <LocatorT, ReadT>(locator: ProviderToken<LocatorT> | string, opts: { descendants?: boolean; read: ProviderToken<ReadT>; debugName?: string; }): Signal<ReadT | undefined>;
  required: {
    <LocatorT>(locator: ProviderToken<LocatorT> | string, opts?: { descendants?: boolean; read?: undefined; debugName?: string; }): Signal<LocatorT>;
    <LocatorT, ReadT>(locator: ProviderToken<LocatorT> | string, opts: { descendants?: boolean; read: ProviderToken<ReadT>; debugName?: string; }): Signal<ReadT>;

    descendants (boolean): Whether to search the entire component subtree.
    read (any): The token to read (e.g., ElementRef, TemplateRef).
    static (boolean): If true, the query is resolved after the first change detection cycle.
    debugName (string): Optional name for debugging.

Returns:
  The matched element/directive or a Signal thereof. Returns undefined if not found unless 'required' is used.

UpgradeAdapter:
  constructor(ng2AppModule: Type<any>, compilerOptions?: CompilerOptions | undefined)
    - Initializes the UpgradeAdapter with the root Angular 2 module and optional compiler options.

  bootstrap(element: Element, modules?: any[], config?: IAngularBootstrapConfig): UpgradeAdapterRef
    - Boots up the Angular 2 application within a specified DOM element.
    - Parameters:
      - element: The DOM element to bootstrap the Angular 2 application into.
      - modules: Optional array of Angular 1 modules to bootstrap with.
      - config: Optional configuration object for bootstrapping.
    - Returns: An UpgradeAdapterRef instance.

  downgradeNg2Component(component: Type<any>): Function
    - Creates a downgrade function for an Angular 2 component to be used in Angular 1.
    - Parameters:
      - component: The Angular 2 component class.
    - Returns: A function that registers the component in Angular 1.

    - Creates a downgrade function for an Angular 2 provider (service) to be used in Angular 1.
    - Parameters:
      - token: The token for the Angular 2 provider.
    - Returns: A function that registers the provider in Angular 1.

    - Registers the adapter for use in Angular 1 tests.

    - Returns: An UpgradeAdapterRef instance.

    - Parameters:
      - name: The name of the Angular 1 component.
    - Returns: The Angular 2 component type.

    - Upgrades an Angular 1 provider to be injectable in Angular 2.
    - Parameters:
      - name: The name of the Angular 1 provider.
      - options: Optional configuration, e.g., to specify an alias token.

UpgradeAdapterRef:
  dispose(): void
    - Disposes of the adapter and cleans up resources.

  ng1Injector: IInjectorService
    - Reference to the Angular 1 injector.

  ng1RootScope: IRootScopeService
    - Reference to the Angular 1 root scope.

  ng2Injector: Injector
    - Reference to the Angular 2 injector.

  ng2ModuleRef: NgModuleRef<any>
    - Reference to the Angular 2 NgModuleRef.

  ready(fn: (upgradeAdapterRef: UpgradeAdapterRef) => void): void
    - Registers a callback function to be executed when the adapter is ready.
    - Parameters:
      - fn: The callback function, receiving the UpgradeAdapterRef.

VERSION: Version
  - Represents the version of the @angular/upgrade package.
