```
TITLE: Browser Web APIs Patched by Zone.js
DESCRIPTION: Lists standard browser Web APIs that are patched by Zone.js to enable zone-aware execution. It details the patch mechanism (Wrap, MacroTask, MicroTask, EventTask) for each API, providing insights into how Zone.js integrates with the browser's asynchronous operations and event handling.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/packages/zone.js/STANDARD-APIS.md#_snippet_0

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Browser Web APIs:

setTimeout/clearTimeout
  - Patch Mechanism: MacroTask
  - Others: app can get handlerId, interval, args, isPeriodic(false) through task.data

setImmediate/clearImmediate
  - Patch Mechanism: MacroTask
  - Others: same with setTimeout

setInterval/clearInterval
  - Patch Mechanism: MacroTask
  - Others: isPeriodic is true, so setInterval will not trigger onHasTask callback

requestAnimationFrame/cancelAnimationFrame
  - Patch Mechanism: MacroTask

mozRequestAnimationFrame/mozCancelAnimationFrame
  - Patch Mechanism: MacroTask

webkitRequestAnimationFrame/webkitCancelAnimationFrame
  - Patch Mechanism: MacroTask

alert
  - Patch Mechanism: wrap

prompt
  - Patch Mechanism: wrap

confirm
  - Patch Mechanism: wrap

Promise
  - Patch Mechanism: MicroTask

EventTarget
  - Patch Mechanism: EventTask
  - Details: see below Event Target for more details

HTMLElement on properties
  - Patch Mechanism: EventTask
  - Details: see below on properties for more details

XMLHttpRequest.send/abort
  - Patch Mechanism: MacroTask

XMLHttpRequest on properties
  - Patch Mechanism: EventTask

IDBIndex on properties
  - Patch Mechanism: EventTask

IDBRequest on properties
  - Patch Mechanism: EventTask

IDBOpenDBRequest on properties
  - Patch Mechanism: EventTask

IDBDatabaseRequest on properties
  - Patch Mechanism: EventTask

IDBTransaction on properties
  - Patch Mechanism: EventTask

IDBCursor on properties
  - Patch Mechanism: EventTask

WebSocket on properties
  - Patch Mechanism: EventTask

MutationObserver
  - Patch Mechanism: wrap

WebkitMutationObserver
  - Patch Mechanism: wrap

FileReader
  - Patch Mechanism: wrap

registerElement
  - Patch Mechanism: wrap
```

TITLE: Angular Input Decorator and Function API
DESCRIPTION: Documents the `@Input` decorator and `input` function for defining input properties in Angular components, including options for aliasing, transformation, and required inputs.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/core/index.api.md#_snippet_34

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Input Decorator:
  @Input(arg?: string | Input)
    - Decorator to mark a class property as an input property.
    - Parameters:
      - arg: Optional string alias for the input property, or an Input configuration object.
        - alias?: string
          - The alias name for the input property.
        - required?: boolean
          - Marks the input property as required.
        - transform?: (value: any) => any
          - A function to transform the input value before it's set.

Input Function:
  const input: InputFunction
    - Function to create input signals.
    - Signatures:
      - <T>(): InputSignal<T | undefined>
        - Creates an input signal without an initial value.
      - <T>(initialValue: T, opts?: InputOptionsWithoutTransform<T>): InputSignal<T>
        - Creates an input signal with an initial value and no transform.
      - <T>(initialValue: undefined, opts: InputOptionsWithoutTransform<T>): InputSignal<T | undefined>
        - Creates an input signal with an undefined initial value and no transform.
      - <T, TransformT>(initialValue: T, opts: InputOptionsWithTransform<T, TransformT>): InputSignalWithTransform<T, TransformT>
        - Creates an input signal with an initial value and a transform function.
      - <T, TransformT>(initialValue: undefined, opts: InputOptionsWithTransform<T | undefined, TransformT>): InputSignalWithTransform<T | undefined, TransformT>
        - Creates an input signal with an undefined initial value and a transform function.

    required:
      - Property to create required input signals.
      - Signatures:
        - <T>(opts?: InputOptionsWithoutTransform<T>): InputSignal<T>
          - Creates a required input signal without a transform.
        - <T, TransformT>(opts: InputOptionsWithTransform<T, TransformT>): InputSignalWithTransform<T, TransformT>
          - Creates a required input signal with a transform.

InputOptions:
  interface InputOptions<T, TransformT>
    - Configuration options for input signals.
    - Properties:
      - alias?: string
        - Alias for the input property.
      - debugName?: string
        - Debugging name for the signal.
      - transform?: (v: TransformT) => T
        - Function to transform the input value.

InputOptionsWithoutTransform:
  type InputOptionsWithoutTransform<T> = Omit<InputOptions<T, T>, 'transform'> & { transform?: undefined }
    - Type for input options without a transform function.

InputOptionsWithTransform:
  type InputOptionsWithTransform<T, TransformT> = Required<Pick<InputOptions<T, TransformT>, 'transform'>> & InputOptions<T, TransformT>
    - Type for input options that require a transform function.

InputSignal:
  interface InputSignal<T> extends InputSignalWithTransform<T, T>
    - Represents an input signal without a transform.

InputSignalWithTransform:
  interface InputSignalWithTransform<T, TransformT> extends Signal<T>
    - Represents an input signal that may have a transform function.
    - Properties:
      - [SIGNAL]: InputSignalNode<T, TransformT>
        - Internal signal node.
      - [ɵINPUT_SIGNAL_BRAND_READ_TYPE]: T
        - Internal type branding for read operations.
      - [ɵINPUT_SIGNAL_BRAND_WRITE_TYPE]: TransformT
        - Internal type branding for write operations.

```

TITLE: Angular UserService for HTTP Requests
DESCRIPTION: An injectable Angular service encapsulating data access logic. It injects HttpClient to make GET requests to an API endpoint, returning an Observable of a User object. This promotes reusability and separation of concerns.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/guide/http/making-requests.md#_snippet_20

LANGUAGE: ts
CODE:
```
@Injectable({providedIn: 'root'})
export class UserService {
  private http = inject(HttpClient);

  getUser(id: string): Observable<User> {
    return this.http.get<User>(`/api/user/${id}`);
  }
}

      - Checks if the animation has started.
    play(): void
      - Starts the animation playback.
    reset(): void
      - Resets the animation player to its initial state.
  Properties:
    currentSnapshot: ɵStyleDataMap
      - The current state snapshot of the animation.
    delay: number
      - The delay before the animation starts.
    duration: number
      - The total duration of the animation.
    easing: string
      - The easing function applied to the animation.
    element: any
      - The DOM element being animated.
    keyframes: Array<ɵStyleDataMap>
      - The keyframes defining the animation steps.
    previousPlayers: any[]
      - An array of previously played animation players.
    previousStyles: ɵStyleDataMap
      - The styles of the element before the animation started.
```

TITLE: Angular Iterable Change Detection API
DESCRIPTION: Documents interfaces for tracking changes in iterable collections, including records of individual item changes and the overall changes within a collection.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/core/index.api.md#_snippet_36

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
IterableChangeRecord:
  interface IterableChangeRecord<V>
    - Represents a single change record for an item in an iterable.
    - Properties:
      - currentIndex: number | null
        - The current index of the item in the collection.
      - item: V
        - The item itself.
      - previousIndex: number | null
        - The previous index of the item in the collection.
      - trackById: any
        - The unique identifier for tracking the item.

IterableChanges:
  interface IterableChanges<V>
    - Represents the collection of changes detected in an iterable.
    - Methods:
      - forEachAddedItem(fn: (record: IterableChangeRecord<V>) => void): void
        - Iterates over each added item record.
      - forEachIdentityChange(fn: (record: IterableChangeRecord<V>) => void): void
        - Iterates over items whose identity has changed.
      - forEachItem(fn: (record: IterableChangeRecord<V>) => void): void
        - Iterates over all items in the collection.
      - forEachMovedItem(fn: (record: IterableChangeRecord<V>) => void): void
        - Iterates over each moved item record.
      - forEachOperation(fn: (record: IterableChangeRecord<V>, previousIndex: number | null, currentIndex: number | null) => void): void
        - Iterates over all operations (add, remove, move) with indices.
      - forEachPreviousItem(fn: (record: IterableChangeRecord<V>) => void): void
        - Iterates over each item from the previous collection state.
      - forEachRemovedItem(fn: (record: IterableChangeRecord<V>) => void): void
        - Iterates over each removed item record.

IterableDiffer:
  interface IterableDiffer<V>
    - Interface for a differ that tracks changes in iterable collections.

```

TITLE: ViewChild and ViewChildren Decorators API
DESCRIPTION: APIs for querying and accessing elements or directives within a component's template. ViewChild selects a single element, while ViewChildren selects multiple.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/core/index.api.md#_snippet_95

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
ViewChildDecorator:
  (selector: ProviderToken<unknown> | Function | string, opts?: { read?: any; static?: boolean }): any;
    - Decorator to get a reference to a single component, directive, or DOM element.
    - Parameters:
      - selector: The selector for the element or directive (e.g., component class, string template name).
      - opts: Optional configuration object.
        - read: Specifies the token to read the dependency from (e.g., ElementRef, TemplateRef).
        - static: If true, resolves the query before change detection runs (only for static queries).

ViewChildFunction:
  <LocatorT, ReadT>(locator: ProviderToken<LocatorT> | string, opts: { read: ProviderToken<ReadT>; debugName?: string }): Signal<ReadT | undefined>;
    - Function-based API to get a signal for a single element/directive, allowing specific token reading.
    - Parameters:
      - locator: The selector for the element or directive.
      - opts: Configuration object.
        - read: The token to read the dependency from.
        - debugName: Optional name for debugging.
    - Returns: A Signal that emits the resolved value or undefined.

  <LocatorT>(locator: ProviderToken<LocatorT> | string, opts?: { debugName?: string }): Signal<LocatorT | undefined>;
    - Function-based API to get a signal for a single element/directive.
    - Parameters:
      - locator: The selector for the element or directive.
      - opts: Optional configuration object.
        - debugName: Optional name for debugging.
    - Returns: A Signal that emits the resolved value or undefined.

  required:
    <LocatorT>(locator: ProviderToken<LocatorT> | string, opts?: { debugName?: string }): Signal<LocatorT>;
      - Function-based API to get a required signal for a single element/directive.
      - Parameters:
        - locator: The selector for the element or directive.
        - opts: Optional configuration object.
          - debugName: Optional name for debugging.
      - Returns: A Signal that emits the resolved value (throws if not found).
    <LocatorT, ReadT>(locator: ProviderToken<LocatorT> | string, opts: { read: ProviderToken<ReadT>; debugName?: string }): Signal<ReadT>;
      - Function-based API to get a required signal for a single element/directive, allowing specific token reading.
      - Parameters:
        - locator: The selector for the element or directive.
        - opts: Configuration object.
          - read: The token to read the dependency from.
          - debugName: Optional name for debugging.
      - Returns: A Signal that emits the resolved value (throws if not found).

ViewChildrenDecorator:
  (selector: ProviderToken<unknown> | Function | string, opts?: { read?: any; emitDistinctChangesOnly?: boolean }): any;
    - Decorator to get a reference to multiple components, directives, or DOM elements.
    - Parameters:
      - selector: The selector for the elements or directives.
      - opts: Optional configuration object.
        - read: Specifies the token to read the dependency from.
        - emitDistinctChangesOnly: If true, only emits when the array content changes distinctly.

viewChildren<LocatorT>(locator: ProviderToken<LocatorT> | string, opts?: { debugName?: string }): Signal<ReadonlyArray<LocatorT>>;
  - Function-based API to get a signal for multiple elements/directives.
  - Parameters:
    - locator: The selector for the elements or directives.
    - opts: Optional configuration object.
      - debugName: Optional name for debugging.
  - Returns: A Signal that emits an array of resolved values.

viewChildren<LocatorT, ReadT>(locator: ProviderToken<LocatorT> | string, opts: { read: ProviderToken<ReadT>; debugName?: string }): Signal<ReadonlyArray<ReadT>>;
  - Function-based API to get a signal for multiple elements/directives, allowing specific token reading.
  - Parameters:
    - locator: The selector for the elements or directives.
    - opts: Configuration object.
      - read: The token to read the dependency from.
      - debugName: Optional name for debugging.
  - Returns: A Signal that emits an array of resolved values.
```

TITLE: RxJS Patch for Zone Management
DESCRIPTION: Zone.js provides a patch for RxJS to ensure Observables, Subscriptions, and Operators run within the correct zone. This example demonstrates how different zones are captured during observable creation, subscription, and operator execution.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/packages/zone.js/NON-STANDARD-APIS.md#_snippet_8

LANGUAGE: ts
CODE:
```
const constructorZone = Zone.current.fork({name: 'constructor'});
const subscriptionZone = Zone.current.fork({name: 'subscription'});
const operatorZone = Zone.current.fork({name: 'operator'});

let observable;
let subscriber;

constructorZone.run(() => {
  observable = new Observable((_subscriber) => {
    subscriber = _subscriber;
    console.log('current zone when construct observable:', Zone.current.name); // will output constructor.
    return () => {
      console.log('current zone when unsubscribe observable:', Zone.current.name); // will output constructor.
    };
  });
});

subscriptionZone.run(() => {
  observable.subscribe({
    next: () => {
      console.log('current zone when subscription next', Zone.current.name); // will output subscription.
    },
    error: () => {
      console.log('current zone when subscription error', Zone.current.name); // will output subscription.
    },
    complete: () => {
      console.log('current zone when subscription complete', Zone.current.name); // will output subscription.
    },
  });
});

operatorZone.run(() => {
  observable.map(() => {
    console.log('current zone when map operator', Zone.current.name); // will output operator.
  });
});
```

----------------------------------------

TITLE: Angular ViewContainerRef API
DESCRIPTION: Defines the API for ViewContainerRef, an abstract class responsible for managing views within a container. It provides methods for creating, detaching, inserting, moving, and removing views, along with accessing its element and injector.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/core/index.api.md#_snippet_98

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
abstract class ViewContainerRef {
    // Creates a component and inserts it into this container.
    abstract createComponent<C>(componentFactory: ComponentFactory<C>, index?: number, injector?: Injector, projectableNodes?: any[][], environmentInjector?: EnvironmentInjector | NgModuleRef<any>, directives?: (Type<unknown> | DirectiveWithBindings<unknown>)[], bindings?: Binding[]): ComponentRef<C>;
    
    // Creates an embedded view based on a TemplateRef and inserts it into this container.
    abstract createEmbeddedView<C>(templateRef: TemplateRef<C>, context?: C, options?: {
        index?: number;
        injector?: Injector;
    }): EmbeddedViewRef<C>;
    abstract createEmbeddedView<C>(templateRef: TemplateRef<C>, context?: C, index?: number): EmbeddedViewRef<C>;
    
    // Detaches a view from the container.
    abstract detach(index?: number): ViewRef | null;
    
    // Gets the host element of the view container.
    abstract get element(): ElementRef;
    
    // Gets a view by its index.
    abstract get(index: number): ViewRef | null;
    
    // Gets the index of a view within the container.
    abstract indexOf(viewRef: ViewRef): number;
    
    // Gets the injector of the view container.
    abstract get injector(): Injector;
    
    // Inserts a view into the container at a specified index.
    abstract insert(viewRef: ViewRef, index?: number): ViewRef;
    
    // Gets the number of views in the container.
    abstract get length(): number;
    
    // Moves a view to a new index within the container.
    abstract move(viewRef: ViewRef, currentIndex: number): ViewRef;
    
    // Gets the parent injector of the view container (deprecated).
    abstract get parentInjector(): Injector;
    
    // Removes a view from the container.
    abstract remove(index?: number): void;
}
```

TITLE: In-Memory Web API URL Parsing (`parseRequestUrl`)
DESCRIPTION: Explains the `parseRequestUrl` function, its role in parsing request URLs into `ParsedRequestUrl` objects, default parsing logic based on configuration, and how to provide a custom implementation.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/packages/misc/angular-in-memory-web-api/README.md#_snippet_8

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
In-Memory Web API URL Parsing (`parseRequestUrl`):

The `parseRequestUrl` parses the request URL into a `ParsedRequestUrl` object, which guides the in-memory web api processing.

Default parsing depends on `config`: `apiBase`, `host`, and `urlRoot`. The actual api base segment values are ignored; only the number of segments matters.

Default Parsing Examples:
* For `apiBase=undefined` and `url='http://localhost/api/customers/42'`:
    ```ts
    {apiBase: 'api/', collectionName: 'customers', id: '42', ...}
    ```
* For `apiBase='some/api/root/'` and `url='http://localhost/some/api/root/customers'`:
    ```ts
    { apiBase: 'some/api/root/', collectionName: 'customers', id: undefined, ... }
    ```
* For `apiBase='/'` and `url='http://localhost/customers'`:
    ```ts
    { apiBase: '/', collectionName: 'customers', id: undefined, ... }
    ```

Custom `parseRequestUrl`:
You can override the default parser by implementing a `parseRequestUrl` method in your `InMemoryDbService`. Your method receives the `url` string and `requestInfoUtils`. It must return a `ParsedRequestUrl` object or `null`|`undefined` to use the default parser.

Example signature for custom parser:
```ts
parseRequestUrl(url: string, requestInfoUtils: RequestInfoUtilities): ParsedRequestUrl | null | undefined;
```
```

TITLE: Angular Router Events
DESCRIPTION: Defines various events emitted by the Angular Router during the navigation lifecycle. These events provide insights into the state of navigation, such as starting, ending, or skipping.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/router/index.api.md#_snippet_16

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
```
export enum EventType {
    NavigationStart = 0,
    NavigationEnd = 1,
    NavigationCancel = 2,
    NavigationError = 3,
    RoutesRecognized = 4,
    RoutesChanged = 5,
    ChildActivationStart = 6,
    ChildActivationEnd = 7,
    ActivationStart = 8,
    ActivationEnd = 9,
    ResolveStart = 10,
    ResolveEnd = 11,
    NavigationSkipped = 12
}

export abstract class RouterEvent {
    // (undocumented)
    abstract readonly type: EventType;
    // (undocumented)
    toString(): string;
}

export class NavigationStart extends RouterEvent {
    constructor(
    id: number,
    url: string,
    navigationTrigger?: NavigationTrigger,
    restoredState?: { [k: string]: any; navigationId: number; } | null);
    navigationTrigger?: NavigationTrigger;
    restoredState?: { [k: string]: any; navigationId: number; } | null;
    // (undocumented)
    toString(): string;
    // (undocumented)
    readonly type = EventType.NavigationStart;
}

export class ResolveStart extends RouterEvent {
    constructor(
    id: number,
    url: string,
    urlAfterRedirects: string,
    state: RouterStateSnapshot);
    // (undocumented)
    state: RouterStateSnapshot;
    // (undocumented)
    toString(): string;
    // (undocumented)
    readonly type = EventType.ResolveStart;
    // (undocumented)
    urlAfterRedirects: string;
}

export class ResolveEnd extends RouterEvent {
    constructor(
    id: number,
    url: string,
    urlAfterRedirects: string,
    state: RouterStateSnapshot);
    // (undocumented)
    state: RouterStateSnapshot;
    // (undocumented)
    toString(): string;
    // (undocumented)
    readonly type = EventType.ResolveEnd;
    // (undocumented)
    urlAfterRedirects: string;
}

export class NavigationSkipped extends RouterEvent {
    readonly type = EventType.NavigationSkipped;
}

```

TITLE: Create Angular Resource for Async Data Fetching
DESCRIPTION: Demonstrates creating an Angular `Resource` to fetch user data reactively based on a `userId` signal. It shows how to define `params` and `loader` for asynchronous operations and how to derive computed signals from the resource's value.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/guide/signals/resource.md#_snippet_0

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
```
import {resource, Signal, computed} from '@angular/core';

const userId: Signal<string> = getUserId();

const userResource = resource({
  // Define a reactive computation.
  // The params value recomputes whenever any read signals change.
  params: () => ({id: userId()}),

  // Define an async loader that retrieves data.
  // The resource calls this function every time the `params` value changes.
  loader: ({params}) => fetchUser(params),
});

// Create a computed signal based on the result of the resource's loader function.
const firstName = computed(() => userResource.value().firstName);
```

TITLE: Angular HttpClient: options Method
DESCRIPTION: Defines the signature for making HTTP OPTIONS requests using Angular's HttpClient. It supports various configurations for headers, parameters, and response observation, returning an Observable of the response body or the full response.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/common/http/index.api.md#_snippet_15

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
HttpClient.options(url: string, options?: { ... }): Observable<HttpResponse<T>> | Observable<Object>;

  - **Description**: Makes an HTTP OPTIONS request to the specified URL.
  - **Parameters**:
    - `url`: The URL to which the request is sent.
    - `options`: An object containing configuration options for the request. This can include:
      - `headers`: HttpHeaders or a record of string headers.
      - `context`: HttpContext for request-level context.
      - `observe`: Specifies how to observe the response ('body' by default).
      - `params`: HttpParams or a record of query parameters.
      - `reportProgress`: Whether to report progress events.
      - `responseType`: The type of the response body ('json' by default).
      - `withCredentials`: Whether to send credentials with the request.
      - `credentials`: RequestCredentials for authentication.
      - `keepalive`: Whether to keep the connection alive.
      - `priority`: RequestPriority for request prioritization.
      - `cache`: RequestCache configuration.
      - `mode`: RequestMode for the request.
      - `redirect`: RequestRedirect policy.
      - `referrer`: The referrer URL.
      - `integrity`: The Subresource Integrity value.
      - `timeout`: Request timeout in milliseconds.
  - **Returns**: An Observable that emits the response. The type depends on the `observe` and `responseType` options. Can be `HttpResponse<T>` or `Object`.

XtbTranslationParser:
  analyze(filePath: string, contents: string): ParseAnalysis<XmlTranslationParserHint>
    - Analyzes the content of an XTB file.
    - Parameters:
      - filePath: The path to the translation file.
      - contents: The content of the translation file.
    - Returns: A ParseAnalysis object containing hints for parsing.

  parse(filePath: string, contents: string, hint: XmlTranslationParserHint): ParsedTranslationBundle

    - Parameters:

      - contents: The content of the translation file.

    - Returns: A ParsedTranslationBundle containing the extracted messages.

```
TITLE: Configure NgOptimizedImage Breakpoints
DESCRIPTION: Customize the default responsive image breakpoints used by NgOptimizedImage. This is achieved by providing a custom `IMAGE_CONFIG` object with a `breakpoints` array to the Angular dependency injection system.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/guide/image-optimization.md#_snippet_12

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
```
import { IMAGE_CONFIG } from '@angular/common';

// ...

providers: [
  {
    provide: IMAGE_CONFIG,
    useValue: {
      breakpoints: [16, 48, 96, 128, 384, 640, 750, 828, 1080, 1200, 1920]
    }
  },
]
```

TITLE: Angular SSR/SSG API Documentation
DESCRIPTION: API reference for Angular's Server-Side Rendering (SSR) and Static Site Generation (SSG) features, covering route configuration, rendering modes, parameter generation, and fallback mechanisms.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/guide/ssr.md#_snippet_9

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Angular SSR/SSG Route Configuration:

ServerRoute:
  An interface defining server-side route configurations.

  Properties:
    path: string
      The route path pattern (e.g., 'user/:id', 'posts').
    renderMode: RenderMode
      Specifies how the route should be rendered. See RenderMode enum.
    getPrerenderParams?: () => Promise<Array<{ [key: string]: string }>>
      (Optional) A function that returns a Promise resolving to an array of parameter objects.
      Each object maps route parameter names to their values, defining which specific routes to prerender.
      Must be used with RenderMode.Prerender.
      Can use Angular's `inject` function synchronously.
    fallback?: PrerenderFallback
      (Optional) Defines the fallback strategy for paths not prerendered.
      Applies only when `renderMode` is `RenderMode.Prerender`.

RenderMode:
  An enum specifying the rendering mode for a route.

  Values:
    Prerender: Prerenders the route at build time.
    Universal: Renders the route on the server for each request.

PrerenderFallback:
  An enum specifying fallback strategies when a prerendered path is requested but not found.

  Values:
    Server: Falls back to server-side rendering (default).
    Client: Falls back to client-side rendering.
    None: No fallback; Angular will not handle requests for unprerendered paths.

Related API:

redirectTo: string | ((url: string) => string) | { redirectTo: string, pathMatch: 'full' | 'prefix' }
  Property within Angular's route configurations used for defining redirects.
  When used with SSR/SSG, the behavior differs: SSR uses HTTP redirects, SSG uses `<meta http-equiv=""refresh"">`.

inject(token: Type<T> | InjectionToken<T>): T
  Angular function to retrieve a dependency instance.
  Must be used synchronously within `getPrerenderParams` or other build-time contexts.
  Cannot be invoked within asynchronous callbacks or after `await` statements.
  For asynchronous injection contexts, use `runInInjectionContext`.

runInInjectionContext(context: Injector, fn: () => R): R
  Runs a function within a specified injection context.
  Useful for using `inject` in asynchronous operations or callbacks where the context is not automatically provided.

```

TITLE: Angular Querying Mechanisms
DESCRIPTION: Defines interfaces and classes for querying and managing lists of elements, typically used in DOM manipulation or component queries. `Query` specifies query parameters, while `QueryList` manages a dynamic list of query results and their changes.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/core/index.api.md#_snippet_79

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
export interface Query {
    descendants: boolean;
    emitDistinctChangesOnly: boolean;
    first: boolean;
    isViewQuery: boolean;
    read: any;
    selector: any;
    static?: boolean;
}
  - Interface defining parameters for querying elements or components.
  - `descendants`: Whether to query descendants.
  - `emitDistinctChangesOnly`: Whether to emit only when changes are distinct.
  - `first`: Whether to return only the first matching element.
  - `isViewQuery`: Indicates if it's a view query.
  - `read`: Specifies a token to read the value from the queried element.
  - `selector`: The selector to match elements.
  - `static`: Whether the query is static (evaluated at creation time).

export abstract class Query {}
  - Abstract base class for query definitions.

export class QueryList<T> implements Iterable<T> {
    [Symbol.iterator]: () => Iterator<T>;
    constructor(_emitDistinctChangesOnly?: boolean);
    get changes(): Observable<any>;
    destroy(): void;
    readonly dirty = true;
    filter<S extends T>(predicate: (value: T, index: number, array: readonly T[]) => value is S): S[];
    filter(predicate: (value: T, index: number, array: readonly T[]) => unknown): T[];
    find(fn: (item: T, index: number, array: T[]) => boolean): T | undefined;
    readonly first: T;
    forEach(fn: (item: T, index: number, array: T[]) => void): void;
    get(index: number): T | undefined;
    readonly last: T;
    readonly length: number;
    map<U>(fn: (item: T, index: number, array: T[]) => U): U[];
    notifyOnChanges(): void;
    reduce<U>(fn: (prevValue: U, curValue: T, curIndex: number, array: T[]) => U, init: U): U;
    reset(resultsTree: Array<T | any[]>, identityAccessor?: (value: T) => unknown): void;
    setDirty(): void;
    some(fn: (value: T, index: number, array: T[]) => boolean): boolean;
    toArray(): T[];
    toString(): string;
}
  - Represents a dynamic list of query results.
  - `changes`: An Observable that emits when the list of results changes.
  - `destroy()`: Cleans up resources associated with the QueryList.
  - `dirty`: A flag indicating if the list needs to be updated.
  - `filter()`: Filters the list based on a predicate function.
  - `find()`: Finds the first element matching a predicate.
  - `first`: The first element in the list.
  - `forEach()`: Iterates over the list elements.
  - `get()`: Retrieves an element by index.
  - `last`: The last element in the list.
  - `length`: The number of elements in the list.
  - `map()`: Transforms each element in the list.
  - `notifyOnChanges()`: Manually triggers change notification.
  - `reduce()`: Reduces the list to a single value.
  - `reset()`: Resets the list with new results.
  - `setDirty()`: Marks the list as dirty.
  - `some()`: Checks if at least one element satisfies a condition.
  - `toArray()`: Converts the QueryList to a standard array.
```

TITLE: NodeJS APIs Patched by Zone.js
DESCRIPTION: Details the Node.js specific APIs that are patched by Zone.js, including their patch mechanism (MacroTask, Microtask, EventTask) and any specific notes on how they are handled. This covers timers, process scheduling, Promises, EventEmitter, crypto, and fs.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/packages/zone.js/STANDARD-APIS.md#_snippet_3

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
NodeJSAPIPatching:
  Description: Zone.js patching mechanisms for various Node.js APIs.
  APIs:
    setTimeout/clearTimeout:
      PatchMechanism: MacroTask
      Details: App can get handlerId, interval, args, isPeriodic(false) through task.data.
    setImmediate/clearImmediate:
      PatchMechanism: MacroTask
      Details: Same as setTimeout.
    setInterval/clearInterval:
      PatchMechanism: MacroTask
      Details: isPeriodic is true, so setInterval will not trigger onHasTask callback.
    process.nextTick:
      PatchMechanism: Microtask
      Details: isPeriodic is true, so setInterval will not trigger onHasTask callback.
    Promise:
      PatchMechanism: MicroTask
      Details: Promises are patched for asynchronous tracking.
    EventEmitter:
      PatchMechanism: EventTask
      Details: All APIs inheriting EventEmitter are patched as EventTask. Methods like addEventListener, prependEventListener, and on are patched once as EventTasks. removeEventListener and removeAllListeners remove these EventTasks.
    crypto:
      PatchMechanism: MacroTask
      Details: Crypto operations are patched.
    fs:
      PatchMechanism: MacroTask
      Details: All asynchronous methods of the fs module are patched.
```

TITLE: Lifecycle Hooks Implementation Example

CODE:
```
class BaseClass implements OnInit {

}

class MyClass extends BaseClass /* Oh noes! Does not implement OnInit */ {
  // BaseClass#ngOnInit is never called!
}

```
TITLE: Meta Tag Management API
DESCRIPTION: Provides methods to interact with HTML meta tags within the browser's document. It allows adding, retrieving, updating, and removing meta tags based on selectors.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/platform-browser/index.api.md#_snippet_8

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Meta Class:
  Manages HTML meta tags in the document.

  constructor(_doc: any)
    Initializes the Meta service with the document context.

  addTag(tag: MetaDefinition, forceCreation?: boolean): HTMLMetaElement | null
    Adds a meta tag to the document. If a tag with the same attributes already exists and forceCreation is false, it returns the existing tag.
    Parameters:
      tag: The MetaDefinition object describing the tag to add.
      forceCreation: If true, creates a new tag even if one exists.
    Returns: The newly created or existing HTMLMetaElement, or null if creation failed.

  addTags(tags: MetaDefinition[], forceCreation?: boolean): HTMLMetaElement[]
    Adds multiple meta tags to the document.
    Parameters:
      tags: An array of MetaDefinition objects.
      forceCreation: If true, creates new tags even if duplicates exist.
    Returns: An array of the created or existing HTMLMetaElement objects.

  getTag(attrSelector: string): HTMLMetaElement | null
    Retrieves a single meta tag based on an attribute selector.
    Parameters:
      attrSelector: A CSS-like selector string (e.g., 'name=""description""').
    Returns: The first matching HTMLMetaElement, or null if none found.

  getTags(attrSelector: string): HTMLMetaElement[]
    Retrieves all meta tags matching an attribute selector.
    Parameters:
      attrSelector: A CSS-like selector string.
    Returns: An array of matching HTMLMetaElement objects.

  removeTag(attrSelector: string): void
    Removes the first meta tag that matches the given attribute selector.
    Parameters:
      attrSelector: A CSS-like selector string.

  removeTagElement(meta: HTMLMetaElement): void
    Removes a specific meta tag element from the document.
    Parameters:
      meta: The HTMLMetaElement to remove.

  updateTag(tag: MetaDefinition, selector?: string): HTMLMetaElement | null
    Updates an existing meta tag or adds it if it doesn't exist. If a selector is provided, it targets a specific tag for update.
    Parameters:
      tag: The MetaDefinition object with updated values.
      selector: An optional attribute selector to find the tag to update.
    Returns: The updated or newly created HTMLMetaElement, or null if update failed.
```

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
MetaDefinition Type:
  Defines the structure for meta tag properties.

  Properties:
    charset?: string;
      Specifies the character encoding of the document (e.g., 'UTF-8').
    content?: string;
      The value of the meta tag, often used with 'name' or 'http-equiv'.
    httpEquiv?: string;
      Defines a header or directive (e.g., 'Content-Type', 'refresh').
    id?: string;
      A unique identifier for the meta tag.
    itemprop?: string;
      Schema.org property name.
    name?: string;
      The name of the meta tag (e.g., 'description', 'keywords').
    property?: string;
      Open Graph or other property-based meta tag name.
    scheme?: string;
      Specifies the scheme used to interpret the content.
    url?: string;
      A URL associated with the meta tag.
    [prop: string]: string;
      Allows for any other valid meta tag attribute.
```

----------------------------------------

TITLE: FormRecord Interface API
DESCRIPTION: Represents a dynamic form group where keys are strings and values are controls, allowing for a map-like structure.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/forms/index.api.md#_snippet_30

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
FormRecord<TControl>:
  Extends: FormGroup<{ [key: string]: TControl }>
  Methods:
    addControl(name: string, control: TControl, options?: { emitEvent?: boolean }): void
      - Adds a new control to the record with the given name.
    contains(controlName: string): boolean
      - Checks if a control with the specified name exists in the record.
    getRawValue(): { [key: string]: ɵRawValue<TControl> }
      - Returns the raw, unmasked values of all controls in the record.
    patchValue(value: { [key: string]: ɵValue<TControl> }, options?: { onlySelf?: boolean; emitEvent?: boolean }): void
      - Patches the values of controls in the record.
    registerControl(name: string, control: TControl): TControl
      - Registers an existing control with the record.
    removeControl(name: string, options?: { emitEvent?: boolean }): void
      - Removes a control from the record by its name.
    reset(value?: { [key: string]: ɵValue<TControl> | FormControlState<ɵValue<TControl>> }, options?: { onlySelf?: boolean; emitEvent?: boolean }): void
      - Resets the record and its controls to a new value or initial state.
    setControl(name: string, control: TControl, options?: { emitEvent?: boolean }): void
      - Sets or replaces a control in the record with a new one.
    setValue(value: { [key: string]: ɵRawValue<TControl> }, options?: { onlySelf?: boolean; emitEvent?: boolean }): void
      - Sets the values of all controls in the record.
```

TITLE: HttpResourceFn API
DESCRIPTION: Defines the primary httpResource function and its overloaded signatures for fetching various resource types (default, arrayBuffer, blob, text). It supports fetching by URL or request object, with options for default values and type inference.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/common/http/index.api.md#_snippet_40

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
HttpResourceFn:
  // Fetches a resource using a URL function and options.
  <TResult = unknown>(url: () => string | undefined, options: HttpResourceOptions<TResult, unknown> & { defaultValue: NoInfer<TResult>; }): HttpResourceRef<TResult>;
  <TResult = unknown>(url: () => string | undefined, options?: HttpResourceOptions<TResult, unknown>): HttpResourceRef<TResult | undefined>;
  // Fetches a resource using a request function and options.
  <TResult = unknown>(request: () => HttpResourceRequest | undefined, options: HttpResourceOptions<TResult, unknown> & { defaultValue: NoInfer<TResult>; }): HttpResourceRef<TResult>;
  <TResult = unknown>(request: () => HttpResourceRequest | undefined, options?: HttpResourceOptions<TResult, unknown>): HttpResourceRef<TResult | undefined>;

  // Specific fetchers for different response types:
  arrayBuffer: {
    <TResult = ArrayBuffer>(url: () => string | undefined, options: HttpResourceOptions<TResult, ArrayBuffer> & { defaultValue: NoInfer<TResult>; }): HttpResourceRef<TResult>;
    <TResult = ArrayBuffer>(url: () => string | undefined, options?: HttpResourceOptions<TResult, ArrayBuffer>): HttpResourceRef<TResult | undefined>;
    <TResult = ArrayBuffer>(request: () => HttpResourceRequest | undefined, options: HttpResourceOptions<TResult, ArrayBuffer> & { defaultValue: NoInfer<TResult>; }): HttpResourceRef<TResult>;
    <TResult = ArrayBuffer>(request: () => HttpResourceRequest | undefined, options?: HttpResourceOptions<TResult, ArrayBuffer>): HttpResourceRef<TResult | undefined>;
  };
  blob: {
    <TResult = Blob>(url: () => string | undefined, options: HttpResourceOptions<TResult, Blob> & { defaultValue: NoInfer<TResult>; }): HttpResourceRef<TResult>;
    <TResult = Blob>(url: () => string | undefined, options?: HttpResourceOptions<TResult, Blob>): HttpResourceRef<TResult | undefined>;
    <TResult = Blob>(request: () => HttpResourceRequest | undefined, options: HttpResourceOptions<TResult, Blob> & { defaultValue: NoInfer<TResult>; }): HttpResourceRef<TResult>;
    <TResult = Blob>(request: () => HttpResourceRequest | undefined, options?: HttpResourceOptions<TResult, Blob>): HttpResourceRef<TResult | undefined>;
  };
  text: {
    <TResult = string>(url: () => string | undefined, options: HttpResourceOptions<TResult, string> & { defaultValue: NoInfer<TResult>; }): HttpResourceRef<TResult>;
    <TResult = string>(url: () => string | undefined, options?: HttpResourceOptions<TResult, string>): HttpResourceRef<TResult | undefined>;
    <TResult = string>(request: () => HttpResourceRequest | undefined, options: HttpResourceOptions<TResult, string> & { defaultValue: NoInfer<TResult>; }): HttpResourceRef<TResult>;
    <TResult = string>(request: () => HttpResourceRequest | undefined, options?: HttpResourceOptions<TResult, string>): HttpResourceRef<TResult | undefined>;
  };

```

```
import { ApplicationConfig } from '@angular/core';

    ),
  ]
};

```
TITLE: HttpResourceRequest Interface
DESCRIPTION: Defines the structure for making an HTTP request, including method, URL, headers, body, and various request options like cache, credentials, and timeout.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/common/http/index.api.md#_snippet_43

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
HttpResourceRequest:
  // The request body.
  body?: unknown;
  // Cache mode for the request.
  cache?: RequestCache | (string & {});
  // HTTP context for the request.
  context?: HttpContext;
  // Credentials mode for the request.
  credentials?: RequestCredentials | (string & {});
  // Request headers.
  headers?: HttpHeaders | Record<string, string | ReadonlyArray<string>>;
  // Integrity value for subresource integrity.
  integrity?: string;
  // Keep-alive flag for the connection.
  keepalive?: boolean;
  // HTTP method (e.g., 'GET', 'POST').
  method?: string;
  // Request mode (e.g., 'cors', 'no-cors').
  mode?: RequestMode | (string & {});
  // URL parameters for the request.
  params?: HttpParams | Record<string, string | number | boolean | ReadonlyArray<string | number | boolean>>;
  // Priority of the request.
  priority?: RequestPriority | (string & {});
  // Redirect mode for the request.
  redirect?: RequestRedirect | (string & {});
  // Referrer policy for the request.
  referrer?: string;
  // Flag to report progress during the request.
  reportProgress?: boolean;
  // Request timeout in milliseconds.
  timeout?: number;
  // Cache transfer options.
  transferCache?: { includeHeaders?: string[]; } | boolean;
  // The URL for the request.
  url: string;
  // Flag to include credentials with the request.
  withCredentials?: boolean;

```

TITLE: Angular Router API References
```

  - Configures a global handler for navigation errors.
  - Parameters:

  - Returns: An `ExtraOptions` object for `provideRouter`.

NavigationError
  - Represents an error that occurred during route navigation.
  - Properties:
    - error: The underlying error object.
    - url: The URL that failed to navigate.

Router.events
  - An Observable stream of all router events.
  - Use `filter` to listen for specific event types like `NavigationError`.

  - Navigates to a new route.
  - Returns a promise that resolves to true if navigation is successful, false otherwise.

    - url: The `UrlTree` to redirect to.

```
----------------------------------------

TITLE: Angular Form Patch Value Example (TypeScript)
DESCRIPTION: Demonstrates how to use the patchValue() method in an Angular component to update specific properties of a form model, such as firstName and street address within a nested structure.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/guide/forms/reactive-forms.md#_snippet_17

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
```
import { Component } from '@angular/core';
import { FormBuilder, FormGroup, Validators } from '@angular/forms';

@Component({
  selector: 'app-profile-editor',
  templateUrl: './profile-editor.component.html',
  styleUrls: ['./profile-editor.component.css']
})
export class ProfileEditorComponent {
  profileForm: FormGroup;

  constructor(private fb: FormBuilder) {
    this.profileForm = this.fb.group({
      firstName: ['', Validators.required],
      lastName: [''],
      address: this.fb.group({
        street: [''],
        city: [''],
        state: [''],
        zip: ['']
      })
    });
  }

  updateProfile() {
    // Example: Update first name and street address
    this.profileForm.patchValue({
      firstName: 'Jane',
      address: {
        street: '456 Oak Avenue'
      }
    });
  }
}
```

TITLE: Advanced Concepts: Change Detection Guide
```

Angular Change Detection:

Purpose: To provide a comprehensive understanding of Angular's change detection mechanism, its performance implications, and optimization strategies.

Key Topics Covered:
- Change Detection Cycle: How Angular detects and updates view changes.
- Zone.js Integration: The role of Zone.js in triggering change detection.
- Trigger Conditions: Events and operations that initiate change detection (e.g., user events, HTTP responses, timers).
- Performance Profiling: Techniques and tools for measuring change detection duration.
- Optimization Practices:
  - Using `OnPush` change detection strategy.
  - Immutable data structures.
  - Detaching and reattaching change detectors.
  - Avoiding unnecessary re-renders.
- Common Pitfalls: Identifying and resolving performance bottlenecks related to change detection.

Target Audience:
- Developers seeking to optimize Angular application performance.
- Developers needing a deeper understanding of Angular's internal workings.

Related Concepts:
- Zone.js
- RxJS Observables
- Performance Profiling Tools (e.g., Angular DevTools, browser profilers)

```
TITLE: Update getAllHousingLocations in housing.service.ts
DESCRIPTION: Modifies the getAllHousingLocations function to make an asynchronous GET request to the configured web server using the fetch API. This replaces the previous synchronous data retrieval method.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/tutorials/first-app/steps/14-http/README.md#_snippet_4

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
```
async getAllHousingLocations(): Promise<HousingLocation[]> {
  const response = await fetch(`${this.url}`);
  if (!response.ok) {
    throw new Error('Failed to fetch housing locations');
  }
  return await response.json() ?? [];
}
```

TITLE: Angular Tutorial Configuration (config.json)
DESCRIPTION: Defines the configuration options for Angular embedded tutorials. This JSON file specifies tutorial metadata, source code paths, and presentation types.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/tutorials/README.md#_snippet_0

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
config.json Configuration:
  - title: string (defines the tutorial title used in the tutorial nav)
  - nextTutorial: string (the path of the next tutorial, only in intro/ step)
  - src: string (the relative path to an external directory, which defines the tutorial source code used in the embedded editor)
  - answerSrc: string (the relative path to an external directory, which defines the tutorial answer used in the embedded editor)
  - openFiles: array of strings (an array of files to be open in the editor)
  - type: string (the type denotes how the tutorial will be presented and which components are necessary for that tutorial)
    - cli: tutorial with content and an interactive terminal with the Angular CLI
    - editor: tutorial with code editor, preview, interactive terminal, and console
    - local: disables the embedded editor and shows only the content
    - editor-only: special config for tutorial playground and homepage playground, disables content, shows only embedded editor
```

TITLE: BrowserPlatformLocation API - Angular
DESCRIPTION: Provides an implementation of PlatformLocation for browser environments. It allows access to browser history, location, and hash changes, and provides methods for navigation.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/common/index.api.md#_snippet_1

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
BrowserPlatformLocation
  constructor()
    - Initializes the browser platform location service.
  back(): void
    - Navigates to the previous page in the browser's history.
  forward(): void
    - Navigates to the next page in the browser's history.
  getBaseHrefFromDOM(): string
    - Retrieves the base HREF from the DOM.
  getState(): unknown
    - Returns the current state object associated with the history entry.
  get hash(): string
    - Gets the URL fragment identifier (the part after '#').
  historyGo(relativePosition?: number): void
    - Navigates through the browser's history by a specified relative position.
  get hostname(): string
    - Gets the hostname of the current URL.
  get href(): string
    - Gets the full URL of the current page.
  onHashChange(fn: LocationChangeListener): VoidFunction
    - Registers a listener for hash changes in the URL.
    - Returns a function to unregister the listener.
  onPopState(fn: LocationChangeListener): VoidFunction
    - Registers a listener for browser history navigation events (e.g., back/forward buttons).
    - Returns a function to unregister the listener.
  get pathname(): string
    - Gets the path portion of the current URL.
  set pathname(newPath: string)
    - Sets the path portion of the current URL.
  get port(): string
    - Gets the port number of the current URL.
  get protocol(): string
    - Gets the protocol of the current URL (e.g., 'http:', 'https:').
  pushState(state: any, title: string, url: string): void
    - Adds a new entry to the browser's history stack.
  replaceState(state: any, title: string, url: string): void
    - Replaces the current history entry with a new one.
  get search(): string
    - Gets the query string portion of the current URL (the part after '?').
```

TITLE: Angular Component Harness Setup and Usage Example
DESCRIPTION: Provides a comprehensive example of setting up `HarnessLoader` and `documentRootLoader` in Angular tests. It shows how to load harnesses for components within the fixture and those appended to the document body.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/guide/testing/using-component-harnesses.md#_snippet_4

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
```
let fixture: ComponentFixture<MyDialogButton>;
let loader: HarnessLoader;
let rootLoader: HarnessLoader;

beforeEach(() => {
  fixture = TestBed.createComponent(MyDialogButton);
  loader = TestbedHarnessEnvironment.loader(fixture);
  rootLoader = TestbedHarnessEnvironment.documentRootLoader(fixture);
});

it('loads harnesses', async () => {
  // Load a harness for the bootstrapped component with `harnessForFixture`
  dialogButtonHarness =
    await TestbedHarnessEnvironment.harnessForFixture(fixture, MyDialogButtonHarness);

  // The button element is inside the fixture's root element, so we use `loader`.
  const buttonHarness = await loader.getHarness(MyButtonHarness);

  // Click the button to open the dialog
  await buttonHarness.click();

  // The dialog is appended to `document.body`, outside of the fixture's root element,
  // so we use `rootLoader` in this case.
  const dialogHarness = await rootLoader.getHarness(MyDialogHarness);

  // ... make some assertions
});
```

TITLE: Angular In-memory Web API: HTTP Method Interceptors
DESCRIPTION: Allows overriding default HTTP method handling in the Angular in-memory web API. Implement methods named after HTTP verbs (e.g., `get`, `post`) in your `InMemoryDbService`. These methods receive a `RequestInfo` object containing request details and utility functions. Custom methods should return an `Observable<Response>` or `null`/`undefined` to indicate intervention or delegation.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/packages/misc/angular-in-memory-web-api/README.md#_snippet_11

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Angular In-memory Web API: HTTP Method Interceptors

Override HTTP Methods:
Implement methods named after HTTP verbs (e.g., ""get"", ""post"", ""put"", ""delete"", ""patch"") in your `InMemoryDbService` class. These methods must be all lowercase.

Method Signature:
yourInMemDbService[""httpMethodName""](requestInfo)

Parameters:
- requestInfo: An object containing request data and utility methods.
  - req: Request; // the request object from the client
  - collectionName: string; // calculated from the request url
  - collection: any[]; // the corresponding collection (if found)
  - id: any; // the item `id` (if specified)
  - url: string; // the url in the request
  - utils: RequestInfoUtilities; // helper functions for request analysis and response composition

Return Values:
- Observable<Response>: If the request is handled. Should be a ""cold"" observable.
- null/undefined: If the service should not intervene and continue with default processing.

Example Usage:
// In your InMemoryDbService implementation:
get(requestInfo) {
  // Custom logic to handle GET requests
  // For example, intercepting specific paths or modifying responses
  if (requestInfo.url.endsWith('/heroes')) {
    // ... custom handling ...
    return new Observable(observer => {
      observer.next(new Response(new ResponseOptions({ body: [{ id: 1, name: 'Super Hero' }] })));
      observer.complete();
    });
  }
  // If not handled, return null to let the default API handle it
  return null;
}

Related Concepts:
- `RequestInfo` interface: Defines the structure of the request object passed to interceptor methods.
- `RequestInfoUtilities`: Helper functions available within `RequestInfo` for easier request processing.
```

TITLE: Custom Image Loader Function
DESCRIPTION: Defines a custom loader function that concatenates the source URL with query parameters based on provided configuration. It supports custom CDN features like rounded corners by checking `loaderParams`.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/guide/image-optimization.md#_snippet_20

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
```
const myCustomLoader = (config: ImageLoaderConfig) => {
  let url = `https://example.com/images/${config.src}?`;
  let queryParams = [];
  if (config.width) {
    queryParams.push(`w=${config.width}`);
  }
  if (config.loaderParams?.roundedCorners) {
    queryParams.push('mask=corners&corner-radius=5');
  }
  return url + queryParams.join('&');
};
```

TITLE: AngularJSUrlCodec API
DESCRIPTION: Implements the UrlCodec interface for encoding and decoding URL components, compatible with AngularJS conventions. It handles path, search, and hash encoding/decoding.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/common/upgrade/index.api.md#_snippet_1

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
AngularJSUrlCodec implements UrlCodec:
  areEqual(valA: string, valB: string): boolean
    - Checks if two URL string values are equal.
  decodeHash(hash: string): string
    - Decodes the hash part of a URL.
  decodePath(path: string, html5Mode?: boolean): string
    - Decodes the path part of a URL, optionally considering HTML5 mode.
  decodeSearch(search: string): { [k: string]: unknown }
    - Decodes the search (query parameters) part of a URL into an object.
  encodeHash(hash: string): string
    - Encodes the hash part of a URL.
  encodePath(path: string): string
    - Encodes the path part of a URL.
  encodeSearch(search: string | { [k: string]: unknown }): string
    - Encodes the search (query parameters) part of a URL.
  normalize(href: string): string
    - Normalizes a full URL string.
  normalize(path: string, search: { [k: string]: unknown }, hash: string, baseUrl?: string): string
    - Normalizes URL components into a full URL string.
  parse(url: string, base?: string): { href: string, protocol: string, host: string, search: string, hash: string, hostname: string, port: string, pathname: string }
    - Parses a URL string into its constituent parts.
```

TITLE: HeroService with Dependencies (TypeScript)
DESCRIPTION: An example of a service that depends on other services, specifically `BackendService` and `Logger`. It fetches heroes asynchronously and logs the number of heroes fetched. This illustrates dependency injection within a service.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/guide/di/creating-injectable-service.md#_snippet_1

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
```
import { inject } from ""@angular/core"";

export class HeroService {
  private heroes: Hero[] = [];

  private backend = inject(BackendService);
  private logger = inject(Logger);

  async getHeroes() {
    // Fetch
    this.heroes = await this.backend.getAll(Hero);
    // Log
    this.logger.log(`Fetched ${this.heroes.length} heroes.`);
    return this.heroes;
  }
}
```

TITLE: Route Guards API
DESCRIPTION: Defines interfaces for route guards, which control navigation to and from routes. Guards can be asynchronous and return booleans, UrlTree, or Observables/Promises of these types.
```

CanActivate:
  canActivate(route: ActivatedRouteSnapshot, state: RouterStateSnapshot): MaybeAsync<GuardResult>
    Determines if a route can be activated.

      route: The route snapshot to activate.
      state: The current router state.
    Returns:
      A boolean, UrlTree, Observable, or Promise indicating if activation is allowed.

CanActivateChild:
  canActivateChild(childRoute: ActivatedRouteSnapshot, state: RouterStateSnapshot): MaybeAsync<GuardResult>
    Determines if a child route can be activated.
    Parameters:
      childRoute: The child route snapshot to activate.
      state: The current router state.
    Returns:
      A boolean, UrlTree, Observable, or Promise indicating if child activation is allowed.

CanDeactivate<T>:

    Determines if a component can be deactivated.

      currentRoute: The route snapshot of the current route.
      currentState: The current router state.
      nextState: The next router state.

CanLoad:

```
----------------------------------------

TITLE: HttpClient Request Options and Response Types
DESCRIPTION: Details the various `responseType` options available for HttpClient requests, allowing developers to specify how the server's response should be interpreted. Includes 'json', 'text', 'arraybuffer', and 'blob'.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/guide/http/making-requests.md#_snippet_3

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
HttpClient.get(url: string, options?: { responseType?: 'json' | 'text' | 'arraybuffer' | 'blob' }): Observable<...>
HttpClient.post(url: string, body: any, options?: { responseType?: 'json' | 'text' | 'arraybuffer' | 'blob' }): Observable<...>

// Parameter: responseType
// Type: 'json' | 'text' | 'arraybuffer' | 'blob'
// Description: Specifies the format of the response. Defaults to 'json'.
//   - 'json': Parses the response body as JSON. The generic type argument on the request method determines the expected structure.
//   - 'text': Returns the response body as a string.
//   - 'arraybuffer': Returns the response body as an ArrayBuffer, useful for binary data.
//   - 'blob': Returns the response body as a Blob object, also for binary data.
// Important: The value for `responseType` must be a literal type (e.g., 'text' as const) if the options object is not a literal.

// Example Usage:
// http.get('/data', { responseType: 'text' })
// http.get('/image', { responseType: 'arraybuffer' })
// http.get('/file', { responseType: 'blob' })

// Note on Generic Types:
// The generic type argument (e.g., <Config>) is a type assertion and does not validate the actual data returned by the server.
```

TITLE: IterableDiffer and Change Detection APIs
DESCRIPTION: Provides interfaces and classes for tracking changes in iterable data structures. DefaultIterableDiffer implements IterableDiffer and IterableChanges, allowing efficient detection of additions, removals, and reordering of items in collections.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/core/index.api.md#_snippet_15

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
```
export interface IterableChanges<V> {
    forEachAddedItem(fn: (record: IterableChangeRecord_<V>) => void): void;
    forEachIdentityChange(fn: (record: IterableChangeRecord_<V>) => void): void;
    forEachItem(fn: (record: IterableChangeRecord_<V>) => void): void;
    forEachMovedItem(fn: (record: IterableChangeRecord_<V>) => void): void;
    forEachOperation(fn: (item: IterableChangeRecord<V>, previousIndex: number | null, currentIndex: number | null) => void): void;
    forEachPreviousItem(fn: (record: IterableChangeRecord_<V>) => void): void;
    forEachRemovedItem(fn: (record: IterableChangeRecord_<V>) => void): void;
    readonly length: number;
}

export class DefaultIterableDiffer<V> implements IterableDiffer<V>, IterableChanges<V> {
    constructor(trackByFn?: TrackByFunction<V>);
    // (undocumented)
    check(collection: NgIterable<V>): boolean;
    // (undocumented)
    readonly collection: V[] | Iterable<V> | null;
    // (undocumented)
    diff(collection: NgIterable<V> | null | undefined): DefaultIterableDiffer<V> | null;
    // (undocumented)
    forEachAddedItem(fn: (record: IterableChangeRecord_<V>) => void): void;
    // (undocumented)
    forEachIdentityChange(fn: (record: IterableChangeRecord_<V>) => void): void;
    // (undocumented)
    forEachItem(fn: (record: IterableChangeRecord_<V>) => void): void;
    // (undocumented)
    forEachMovedItem(fn: (record: IterableChangeRecord_<V>) => void): void;
    // (undocumented)
    forEachOperation(fn: (item: IterableChangeRecord<V>, previousIndex: number | null, currentIndex: number | null) => void): void;
    // (undocumented)
    forEachPreviousItem(fn: (record: IterableChangeRecord_<V>) => void): void;
    // (undocumented)
    forEachRemovedItem(fn: (record: IterableChangeRecord_<V>) => void): void;
    // (undocumented)
    get isDirty(): boolean;
    // (undocumented)
    readonly length: number;
    // (undocumented)
    onDestroy(): void;
}
```

TITLE: Publishing Snapshot Builds
DESCRIPTION: Scripts and commands for manually publishing snapshot builds of Angular packages. This allows external participants to test un-merged changes by depending on snapshots created from a Pull Request.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/contributing-docs/building-and-testing-angular.md#_snippet_9

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
Publishing Build Artifacts:

Prerequisites:
- Build packages locally by running `yarn build`.

First-time setup (create GitHub repositories):
- `export TOKEN=[get one from https://github.com/settings/tokens]`
- `CREATE_REPOS=1 ./scripts/ci/publish-build-artifacts.sh [GitHub username]`
  - Requires a GitHub token and creates necessary repositories.

Subsequent snapshots:
- `./scripts/ci/publish-build-artifacts.sh [GitHub username]`
  - Publishes the build snapshot to a branch matching the current branch name, creating it if it doesn't exist.
```

TITLE: Angular Service Worker Core APIs
DESCRIPTION: Provides core functionalities for integrating Angular applications with service workers. This includes registering the service worker, managing push notifications via SwPush, and handling application updates with SwUpdate. It also defines configuration options and event types for various service worker states.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/service-worker/index.api.md#_snippet_0

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
ServiceWorkerModule:
  static register(script: string, options?: SwRegistrationOptions): ModuleWithProviders<ServiceWorkerModule>
    - Registers the service worker for the application.
    - Parameters:
      - script: The path to the service worker script.
      - options: Optional configuration for registration (SwRegistrationOptions).
    - Returns: A ModuleWithProviders object for configuring the Angular module.

provideServiceWorker(script: string, options?: SwRegistrationOptions): EnvironmentProviders
    - A function to provide the service worker functionality as environment providers.
    - Parameters:
      - script: The path to the service worker script.
      - options: Optional configuration for registration (SwRegistrationOptions).
    - Returns: EnvironmentProviders for the application.

SwRegistrationOptions:
  - Abstract class defining options for service worker registration.
  - Properties:
    - enabled?: boolean
      - Whether the service worker is enabled. Defaults to true.
    - registrationStrategy?: string | (() => Observable<unknown>)
      - Strategy for service worker registration. Can be a string ('registerImmediately', 'registerOnStable') or a function returning an Observable.
    - scope?: string
      - The scope for the service worker registration.

SwPush:
  - Service for handling push notifications.
  - Properties:
    - isEnabled: boolean
      - Indicates if the service worker is enabled and push notifications are supported.
    - messages: Observable<object>
      - Observable that emits messages received from the service worker.
    - notificationClicks: Observable<{ action: string; notification: NotificationOptions & { title: string; }; }>
      - Observable that emits when a notification is clicked.
    - notificationCloses: Observable<{ action: string; notification: NotificationOptions & { title: string; }; }>
      - Observable that emits when a notification is closed.
    - pushSubscriptionChanges: Observable<{ oldSubscription: PushSubscription | null; newSubscription: PushSubscription | null; }>
      - Observable that emits when the push subscription changes.
    - subscription: Observable<PushSubscription | null>
      - Observable that emits the current push subscription.
  - Methods:
    - requestSubscription(options: { serverPublicKey: string; }): Promise<PushSubscription>
      - Requests a push notification subscription from the user.
      - Parameters:
        - options: An object containing the server's public key.
      - Returns: A Promise that resolves with the PushSubscription object.
    - unsubscribe(): Promise<void>
      - Unsubscribes from push notifications.
      - Returns: A Promise that resolves when unsubscribed.

SwUpdate:
  - Service for managing application updates.
  - Properties:
    - isEnabled: boolean
      - Indicates if the service worker is enabled and update checks are supported.
    - unrecoverable: Observable<UnrecoverableStateEvent>
      - Observable that emits when an unrecoverable state is detected.
    - versionUpdates: Observable<VersionEvent>
      - Observable that emits events related to version updates.
  - Methods:
    - activateUpdate(): Promise<boolean>
      - Activates a pending service worker update.
      - Returns: A Promise resolving to true if an update was activated, false otherwise.
    - checkForUpdate(): Promise<boolean>
      - Checks for a new version of the application.
      - Returns: A Promise resolving to true if an update is available, false otherwise.

VersionEvent Types:
  - VersionDetectedEvent:
    - type: 'VERSION_DETECTED'
    - version: { hash: string; appData?: object; }
  - VersionReadyEvent:
    - type: 'VERSION_READY'
    - currentVersion: { hash: string; appData?: object; }
    - latestVersion: { hash: string; appData?: object; }
  - VersionInstallationFailedEvent:
    - type: 'VERSION_INSTALLATION_FAILED'
    - error: string
    - version: { hash: string; appData?: object; }
  - NoNewVersionDetectedEvent:
    - type: 'NO_NEW_VERSION_DETECTED'
    - version: { hash: string; appData?: object; }
  - UnrecoverableStateEvent:
    - type: 'UNRECOVERABLE_STATE'
    - reason: string

```

TITLE: Angular Logical Tree with skipSelf and host
DESCRIPTION: Depicts the logical tree with `skipSelf` and `host` applied to `inject`. This example clarifies how `skipSelf` alters the starting point of the search and how `host` defines the search termination point within the injector hierarchy.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/guide/di/hierarchical-dependency-injection.md#_snippet_49

LANGUAGE: html
CODE:
```
<app-root @ApplicationConfig
        @Inject(AnimalService=>""&#x1F433;"")>
  <#VIEW @Provide(AnimalService=""&#x1F994;"")
         @Inject(AnimalService, @Optional)=>""&#x1F994;"">
    <!-- ^^skipSelf starts here,  host stops here^^ -->
    <app-child>
      <#VIEW @Provide(AnimalService=""&#x1F436;"")
             inject(AnimalService, {skipSelf:true, host: true, optional: true})=>""&#x1F994;"">
               <!-- Add skipSelf ^^-->
      </#VIEW>
      </app-child>
  </#VIEW>
</app-root>
```

TITLE: Connected Sorting Example (TypeScript/HTML)
DESCRIPTION: A comprehensive example showcasing connected sorting between multiple drop lists. It includes the HTML structure, component logic, and styling for a functional drag-and-drop interface.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/guide/drag-drop.md#_snippet_6

LANGUAGE: html
CODE:
```
<div class=""container"">
  <div
    cdkDropList
    class=""demo-list""
    (cdkDropListDropped)=""drop($event)""
    [cdkDropListData]=""item""
    *ngFor=""let item of items""
    [id]=""item.id""
    [cdkDropListConnectedTo]=""item.connectedTo""
  >
    @for (subItem of item.subItems; track subItem) {
      <div class=""demo-box""
           cdkDrag
           [cdkDragData]=""subItem"">
        {{subItem.name}}
      </div>
    }
  </div>
</div>
```

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
```
import {
  CdkDragDrop,
  moveItemInArray,
  transferArrayItem,
} from '@angular/cdk/drag-drop';
import {
  Component,
  ChangeDetectionStrategy,
  ChangeDetectorRef,
} from '@angular/core';

/**
 * @title Drag and drop connected sorting
 */
@Component({
  selector: 'cdk-drag-drop-connected-sorting-example',
  templateUrl: 'app.component.html',
  styleUrls: ['app.component.css'],
  changeDetection: ChangeDetectionStrategy.OnPush,
})
export class CdkDragDropConnectedSortingExample {
  items: any[] = [
    {
      id: 'list-1',
      connectedTo: ['list-2'],
      subItems: [
        { name: 'Item 1', id: 1 },
        { name: 'Item 2', id: 2 },
        { name: 'Item 3', id: 3 },
      ],
    },
    {
      id: 'list-2',
      connectedTo: ['list-1'],
      subItems: [
        { name: 'Item 4', id: 4 },
        { name: 'Item 5', id: 5 },
        { name: 'Item 6', id: 6 },
      ],
    },
  ];

  constructor(private cdr: ChangeDetectorRef) {}

  drop(event: CdkDragDrop<any[]>) {
    if (event.previousContainer === event.container) {
      moveItemInArray(
        event.container.data,
        event.previousIndex,
        event.currentIndex
      );
    } else {
      transferArrayItem(
        event.previousContainer.data,
        event.container.data,
        event.previousIndex,
        event.currentIndex
      );
    }
    this.cdr.markForCheck();
  }
}

```

LANGUAGE: css
CODE:
```
.container {
  display: flex;
  flex-direction: row;
  justify-content: space-around;
}

  min-width: 150px;

  flex-grow: 1;
}

```
TITLE: LView/TView.data VARS Section Example
DESCRIPTION: Demonstrates the VARS section of LView and TView.data with a TypeScript example. It highlights how binding values are stored in LView and corresponding property names or metadata in TView.data, illustrating template update mechanisms.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/packages/core/src/render3/VIEW_DATA.md#_snippet_2

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
```
@Component({
  template: `<div title=""{{name}}"">Hello {{name}}!</div>`
})
class MyApp {
  name = 'World';

  static ɵcmp = ɵɵdefineComponent({
    ...,
    decls: 2, // Two DOM Elements.
    vars: 2,   // Two bindings.
    template: function(rf: RenderFlags, ctx: MyApp) {
      if (rf & RenderFlags.Create) {
        ɵɵelementStart(0, 'div');
        ɵɵtext(1);
        ɵɵelementEnd();
      }
      if (rf & RenderFlags.Update) {
        ɵɵproperty('title', ctx.name);
        ɵɵadvance();
        ɵɵtextInterpolate1('Hello ', ctx.name, '!');
      }
      ...
    }
  });
}

  | 11    | `#text()`     | `{type: Element, index: 11, parent: tView.data[10]}`

  | 13    | `'World'`     | `null`
  | ...   | ...           | ...

```
TITLE: Angular Signals: Basic Signal, Computed, and Effect Example
DESCRIPTION: Demonstrates the core Angular Signals API with `signal` for mutable state, `computed` for derived values, and `effect` for side effects. It illustrates how changes propagate and the potential for glitches if not handled properly.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/packages/core/primitives/signals/README.md#_snippet_5

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
```
import { signal, computed, effect } from '@angular/core';

const counter = signal(0);
const evenOrOdd = computed(() => counter() % 2 === 0 ? 'even' : 'odd');
effect(() => console.log(counter() + ' is ' + evenOrOdd()));

counter.set(1);
// Expected output: 0 is even, then 1 is odd (glitch-free)
```

TITLE: Use `protected` for Template-Only Members
DESCRIPTION: Mark class members that are exclusively used within the component's template as `protected`. This clearly defines them as internal implementation details, not part of the component's public API accessible via DI or queries, enhancing encapsulation.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/adev/src/content/best-practices/style-guide.md#_snippet_4

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
```
@Component({
  selector: 'app-user-profile',
  template: `<p>{{ fullName() }}</p>`
})
export class UserProfile {
  firstName = input();
  lastName = input();

  // `fullName` is not part of the component's public API, but is used in the template.
  protected fullName = computed(() => `${this.firstName()} ${this.lastName()}`);
}
```

TITLE: ControlValueAccessor Interface
DESCRIPTION: Defines the interface that components must implement to be integrated with Angular's forms API. It allows custom components to register callbacks for value changes and touch events.
SOURCE: https://github.com/angular/angular/blob/main/goldens/public-api/forms/index.api.md#_snippet_2

LANGUAGE: APIDOC
CODE:
```
ControlValueAccessor:
  registerOnChange(fn: any): void
    - Registers a callback function that is called when the control's value changes.
  registerOnTouched(fn: any): void
    - Registers a callback function that is called when the control is touched.
  setDisabledState?(isDisabled: boolean): void
    - Optional method to enable/disable the control.
  writeValue(obj: any): void
    - Writes a new value to the control. This method is called by the Angular framework to update the form control's value.
